## 小( )学(學)
---
## primary school
### xiǎoxué
---
- **traditional:** 小學
- **definition:** primary school
- **pinyin:** xiǎoxué
- **components:**
  - 小
    - xiǎo
    - small
  - 学(學)
    - xué
    - study; learn; school; knowledge
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 小 (xiǎo, "small") + 学(學) (xué, "study") =
    - a place or institution for small or young students to study, hence 'primary school'.
  - **interpretation:** 小( )学(學) (xiǎoxué, "primary school") refers to the initial stage of formal education, where young children first begin their structured learning. The use of 'small' signifies the early and foundational level of schooling.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )的( )小( )女( )儿(兒)今( )年( )开(開)始( )上( )小( )学(學)。
    - Wǒ de xiǎo nǚ'ér jīnnián kāishǐ shàng xiǎoxué.
    - My little daughter is starting primary school this year.
  - 小( )学(學)的( )课(課)程( )比( )较(較)简(簡)单(單)。
    - Xiǎoxué de kèchéng bǐjiào jiǎndān.
    - The curriculum in primary school is relatively simple.
  - 我( )第( )一( )次( )见(見)他( )是( )在( )小( )学(學)。
    - Wǒ dì yī cì jiàn tā shì zài xiǎoxué.
    - The first time I met him was in primary school.
### 小( )学(學) → 小
- **definition:** small
- **pinyin:** xiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts three small dots arranged symmetrically to represent something small
  - **interpretation:** The character 小(xiǎo, 'small') uses three small strokes to symbolize size or quantity, visually capturing the essence of 'smallness'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小( )猫(貓)很( )可( )爱(愛)。
    - Zhège xiǎo māo hěn kě'ài.
    - This small cat is very cute.
  - 这(這)座( )小( )桥(橋)横(橫)跨( )河( )流( )，连(連)接( )两(兩)岸( )。
    - Zhè zuò xiǎo qiáo héngkuà héliú, liánjiē liǎng àn.
    - This small bridge spans the river, connecting both banks.
  - 请(請)给(給)我( )一( )小( )杯( )水( )。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ yī xiǎo bēi shuǐ.
    - Please give me a small cup of water.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 小](@media/glyph5c0f.png)
### 小( )学(學) → 学(學)
- **traditional:** 學
- **definition:** study; learn; school; knowledge
- **pinyin:** xué
- **components:**
  - 爻
    - yáo
    - double cross
  - 六
    - liù
    - six
  - 𦥑
    - kuk
    - hands around
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 爻 + phonetic 六 ->
    - 𦥑 added ->
    - semantic 子 added ->
    - simplified 六 ->
    - final form
  - **interpretation:** The character 學 (xué, "study") originally combined two phonetic components, 爻 (yáo, "double cross") and 六 (liù, "six"), to represent its sound. Over time, the character evolved with the addition of 𦥑 (components positioned like hands around 爻) and the semantic 子 (zǐ, "child") to specify a child learning or studying, under a cover (冖). In its modern form, 六 is simplified to resemble 冖, which visually merges with the hands around 爻, reflecting the learning process enclosed as children gather to study.
  - **simplification:** "学" is the simplified form of "學." The transformation occurred by merging the visual elements into a compact form, where 冖 serves as a common phonetic and visual element, while the complex structure of 學 was streamlined.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )每( )天( )都( )努( )力( )学(學)习(習)。
    - Tā měitiān dōu nǔlì xuéxí.
    - He studies diligently every day.
  - 我( )在( )北( )京( )大( )学(學)学(學)习(習)中( )文( )。
    - Wǒ zài Běijīng Dàxué xuéxí zhōngwén.
    - I am studying Chinese at Peking University.
  - 这(這)个(個)学(學)校( )有( )很( )多( )优(優)秀( )的( )老( )师(師)。
    - Zhège xuéxiào yǒu hěnduō yōuxiù de lǎoshī.
    - This school has many excellent teachers.
### 小( )学(學) → 学(學) → 爻
- **definition:** double cross
- **pinyin:** yáo
- **components:**
  - 乂
    - yì
    - to govern
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 乂 (yì, "to govern") + 乂 =
    - two stacked 'X' marks representing divination lines
  - **interpretation:** The character 爻(yáo, "divination lines") depicts two crossing lines, resembling 'X' marks, symbolizing the divination lines used in traditional methods. These marks can be interpreted as representing either pairs of yarrow stalks used for divination or bamboo slips used for calculations. Though it might visually resemble 交 (jiāo, "cross") or 駁 (bó, "contradict"), its primary function is depicting the meaningful crossing patterns in divination.
- **examples:**
  - 易( )经(經)卜( )卦( )时(時)，观(觀)察( )爻( )的( )变(變)化( )。
    - Yì jīng bǔ guà shí, guānchá yáo de biànhuà.
    - When consulting the I Ching, one observes the changes of the divination lines.
  - 卦( )中( )的( )每( )一( )个(個)爻( )都( )蕴(蘊)含( )宇( )宙( )奥(奧)秘( )。
    - Guà zhōng de měi yīgè yáo dōu yùnhán yǔzhòu àomì.
    - Every divination line in the hexagram contains the mysteries of the universe.
  - 大( )师(師)解( )读(讀)时(時)，详(詳)细(細)说(說)明( )爻( )的( )象( )征(徵)意( )义(義)。
    - Dàshī jiědú shí, xiángxì shuōmíng yáo de xiàngzhēng yìyì.
    - When the master interprets, he elaborates on the symbolic meaning of the divination lines.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 爻](@media/glyph723b.png)
### 小( )学(學) → 学(學) → 爻 → 乂
- **definition:** to govern
- **pinyin:** yì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a tool (similar to a sickle or a pair of scissors) for mowing or weeding ->
    - used for governing ->
    - final form 乂
  - **interpretation:** The character 乂 originally depicted a tool used for cutting, and by extension, it was associated with governing due to the notion of cutting or managing weeds as a metaphor for ruling effectively. This sense of order is crucial in governance.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)些( )年( )，他( )致( )力( )于(於)地( )方( )的( )治( )理( )。
    - Zhèxiē nián, tā zhìlì yú dìfāng de zhìlǐ.
    - Over the years, he has dedicated himself to local governance.
  - 为(為)民( )者( )，先( )自( )齐(齊)以( )治( )家( )。
    - Wèi mín zhě, xiān zì qí yǐ zhì jiā.
    - Those who govern for the people, first manage their own households.
  - 长(長)者( )都( )希( )望( )后(後)代( )能( )好( )好( )治( )理( )天( )下( )。
    - Zhǎng zhě dōu xīwàng hòudài néng hǎohǎo zhìlǐ tiānxià.
    - The elders hope that future generations can govern the world well.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 乂](@media/glyph4e42.png)
### 小( )学(學) → 学(學) → 六
- **definition:** six
- **pinyin:** liù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Ancient counting symbol ->
    - character for 'six'
  - **interpretation:** 六 (liù, 'six') is a pictogram that may originally have depicted a shed, but was primarily used as an ancient counting symbol. The form resembles primitive tally markings used for numerical purposes.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )六( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Wǒ yǒu liù gè píngguǒ.
    - I have six apples.
  - 这(這)个(個)盒( )子( )可( )以( )放( )六( )瓶( )水( )。
    - Zhè gè hézi kěyǐ fàng liù píng shuǐ.
    - This box can hold six bottles of water.
  - 六( )只(隻)猫(貓)在( )花( )园(園)里(裡)玩( )耍( )。
    - Liù zhī māo zài huāyuán lǐ wánshuǎ.
    - Six cats are playing in the garden.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 六](@media/glyph516d.png)
### 小( )学(學) → 学(學) → 𦥑
- **definition:** hands around
- **pinyin:** kuk
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a pair of hands
  - **interpretation:** The character 𦥑 (kù, "hands") directly represents the image of two hands, embodying the concept through visual depiction. It is a straightforward pictogram, intended to convey the physical form and function of hands.
### 小( )学(學) → 学(學) → 子
- **definition:** child
- **pinyin:** zǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a baby with a large head and spread arms, with legs wrapped in a blanket
  - **interpretation:** The character 子(zǐ, "child") is a pictorial representation of a baby, emphasizing characteristics like a large head and outstretched arms typical of infants, which conveys the essence of a child. This visual element helps infer its meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)小( )子( )很( )调(調)皮( )。
    - Zhè xiǎo zǐ hěn tiáopí.
    - This kid is very naughty.
  - 他( )的( )小( )子( )爱(愛)打( )篮(籃)球( )，每( )天( )都( )锻(鍛)炼(煉)身( )体(體)。
    - Tā de xiǎo zǐ ài dǎ lánqiú, měitiān dōu duànliàn shēntǐ.
    - His child loves playing basketball, and practices every day.
  - 孤( )独(獨)的( )子( )需( )要( )关(關)爱(愛)。
    - Gūdú de zǐ xūyào guān'ài.
    - A lonely child needs care.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 子](@media/glyph5b50.png)

## 浴室
---
## bathroom
### yùshì
---
- **definition:** bathroom
- **pinyin:** yùshì
- **components:**
  - 浴
    - yù
    - to bathe; bath
  - 室
    - shì
    - room; chamber
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 浴 (yù, "to bathe") + 室 (shì, "room") =
    - A room for bathing, hence bathroom.
  - **interpretation:** 浴 (yù, "to bathe") depicts immersion in water for washing or cleansing -> place for this activity. 室 (shì, "room") is an enclosed space -> together they create a space designated for bathing activities.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )在( )浴( )室( )洗( )了( )个(個)澡( )。
    - Wǒ zài yùshì xǐ le gè zǎo.
    - I took a shower in the bathroom.
  - 她( )喜( )欢(歡)在( )浴( )室( )里(裡)唱( )歌( )。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài yùshì lǐ chànggē.
    - She likes to sing in the bathroom.
  - 浴( )室( )里(裡)的( )灯(燈)坏(壞)了( )，需要修理。
    - Yùshì lǐ de dēng huài le, xūyào xiūlǐ.
    - The light in the bathroom is broken and needs repair.
### 浴室 → 浴
- **definition:** to bathe; bath
- **pinyin:** yù
- **components:**
  - 氵
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 谷
    - gǔ
    - valley
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 氵 (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic: 谷 (gǔ, "valley") =
    - valley filled with water ->
    - bathe
  - **interpretation:** The character 浴 (yù, "bathe") combines the semantic component 氵 (shuǐ, "water") indicating relation to liquid and the phonetic component 谷 (gǔ, "valley"). This suggests a place where water collects, such as a valley filled with water, an apt metaphor for bathing.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )在( )浴( )室( )里(裡)洗( )澡( )。
    - Tā zài yùshì lǐ xǐzǎo.
    - He bathes in the bathroom.
  - 黄(黃)昏( )时(時)他( )在( )温(溫)泉( )浴( )池( )中( )沐( )浴( )，忘( )却(卻)一( )天( )烦(煩)恼(惱)。
    - Huánghūn shí tā zài wēnquán yùchí zhōng mùyù, wàngquè yītiān fánnǎo.
    - At dusk, he bathes in the hot spring pool and forgets the troubles of the day.
  - 她( )享( )受( )晨( )浴( )后(後)的( )清( )新( )。
    - Tā xiǎngshòu chén yù hòu de qīngxīn.
    - She enjoys the freshness after her morning bath.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 浴](@media/glyph6d74.png)
### 浴室 → 浴 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字( )中( )偏( )旁( )氵( )，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快( )戏(戲)水( )。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 浴室 → 浴 → 谷
- **definition:** valley
- **pinyin:** gǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts valley: 口 (kǒu, "mouth" or open space) in between two mountain walls represented by near-parallel lines ->
    - original form is 𠔌
  - **interpretation:** The character 谷(gǔ, 'valley') visually represents a valley, with an open space flanked by lines resembling mountains. This aligns with its definition as a valley, a feature of the landscape formed by natural geological processes.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )走( )进(進)了( )幽( )静(靜)的( )谷( )。
    - Tā zǒu jìnle yōujìng de gǔ.
    - He walked into the quiet valley.
  - 清( )晨( )的( )时(時)候( )，薄( )雾(霧)笼(籠)罩( )着(著)谷( )。
    - Qīngchén de shíhòu, bó wù lóngzhào zhe gǔ.
    - In the early morning, a thin mist covered the valley.
  - 山( )谷( )里(裡)回( )荡(盪)着(著)鸟(鳥)鸣(鳴)。
    - Shāngǔ lǐ huídàngzhe niǎomíng.
    - The valley echoes with birdsong.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 谷](@media/glyph8c37.png)
### 浴室 → 室
- **definition:** room; chamber
- **pinyin:** shì
- **components:**
  - 宀
    - mián
    - roof
  - 至
    - zhì
    - arrive
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 宀(“roof”) + 至(phonetic, “arrive”/“this exact spot”) =
    - a house or residence under a roof
  - **interpretation:** The character 室(shì, "room") combines the semantic element 宀(shì, "roof") with the phonetic 至(zhì, "arrive"), symbolizing a covered place where one stops or resides. This interpretation aligns with historical uses of 室 to denote a specific location or dwelling.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )书(書)在( )房( )间(間)里(裏)。
    - Tā de shū zài fángjiān lǐ.
    - His book is in the room.
  - 走( )进(進)这(這)个(個)房( )间(間)，你( )会(會)发(發)现(現)它( )很( )温(溫)馨( )。
    - Zǒujìn zhègè fángjiān, nǐ huì fāxiàn tā hěn wēnxīn.
    - When you enter this room, you will find it very cozy.
  - 会(會)议(議)室( )在( )走( )廊( )的( )尽(盡)头(頭)。
    - Huìyì shì zài zǒuláng de jìntóu.
    - The meeting room is at the end of the corridor.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 室](@media/glyph5ba4.png)
### 浴室 → 室 → 宀
- **definition:** roof
- **pinyin:** mián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a house with four walls ->
    - roof
  - **interpretation:** 宀(mián, "roof") is a pictogram representing a house with four walls. It emphasizes an enclosed space, distinguishing it from similar structures like 广(guǎng, "broad") which depicts a building with three walls. This makes 宀 a logical choice for representing a roof in various characters.
- **examples:**
  - 含( )有( )宀( )的( )汉(漢)字( )代( )表( )家( )的( )温(溫)暖( )。
    - Hán yǒu mián de hànzì dàibiǎo jiā de wēnnuǎn.
    - Chinese characters that include the radical '宀' represent the warmth of home.
  - 屋( )顶(頂)遮( )风(風)挡(擋)雨( )，家( )园(園)散( )发(發)温(溫)馨( )。
    - Wūdǐng zhē fēng dǎng yǔ, jiāyuán sànfā wēnxīn.
    - The roof shields from wind and rain, and the home radiates warmth.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 宀](@media/glyph5b80.png)
### 浴室 → 室 → 至
- **definition:** arrive
- **pinyin:** zhì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts an arrow stuck into the ground ->
    - express arrival or reaching a destination
  - **interpretation:** The image of an arrow embedded in the ground symbolizes reaching a fixed endpoint, evoking the idea of arriving at a particular place.
- **examples:**
  - 火( )车(車)已( )至( )。
    - Huǒchē yǐ zhì.
    - The train has arrived.
  - 从(從)广(廣)州( )出( )发(發)，火( )车(車)已( )至( )目( )的( )地( )。
    - Cóng Guǎngzhōu chūfā, huǒchē yǐ zhì mùdìdì.
    - Departing from Guangzhou, the train has arrived at its destination.
  - 信( )使( )至( )长(長)安( )。
    - Xìnshǐ zhì Cháng'ān.
    - The messenger has arrived in Chang'an.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 至](@media/glyph81f3.png)

## 冲(沖)
---
## rush
### chōng
---
- **traditional:** 沖
- **definition:** rush
- **pinyin:** chōng
- **components:**
  - 氵(水)
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic 中 (zhōng) ->
    - rush of water
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 水 (shuǐ, "water") for its semantic element, conveying the idea of fluid movement, with 中 (zhōng) to provide the phonetic element, approximating the sound 'chōng'. Water naturally rushes or flows, leading to the idea of a rapid movement or 'rush'.
  - **simplification:** 沖 was simplified to 冲 by retaining 中 (zhōng, "middle") as it is, but reducing 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water") to 冲's simpler top-stroke form.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )匆( )匆( )冲(沖)出( )门(門)。
    - Tā cōngcōng chōng chū mén.
    - He rushed out of the door in a hurry.
  - 清( )晨( )的( )海( )浪( )冲(沖)上( )沙( )滩(灘)。
    - Qīngchén de hǎilàng chōng shàng shātān.
    - The morning waves rushed onto the beach.
  - 孩( )子( )们(們)冲(沖)向( )操( )场(場)，欢(歡)呼( )雀( )跃(躍)。
    - Háizimen chōng xiàng cāochǎng, huānhū què yuè.
    - The children rushed to the playground, cheering joyfully.
### 冲(沖) → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字( )中( )偏( )旁( )氵( )，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快( )戏(戲)水( )。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 冲(沖) → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看( )着(著)远(遠)方( )。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房( )间(間)正( )中( )，挂(掛)着(著)一( )幅( )名( )画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 中](@media/glyph4e2d.png)

## shout; cry
### jiào
---
- **definition:** shout; cry
- **pinyin:** jiào
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 丩
    - jiū
    - hook
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic 丩 ->
    - shout
  - **interpretation:** The mouth 口 (kǒu, "mouth") indicates an action related to speaking or making noise, while the phonetic 丩 suggests the sound of shouting or calling. Together, they convey the concept of calling out or shouting.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )叫( )了( )一( )声(聲)，但( )没(沒)有( )人( )回( )答( )。
    - Tā jiào le yī shēng, dàn méiyǒu rén huídá.
    - He shouted, but no one answered.
  - 我( )叫( )他( )来(來)帮(幫)忙( )，他( )马(馬)上( )就( )答( )应(應)了( )。
    - Wǒ jiào tā lái bāngmáng, tā mǎshàng jiù dāyìng le.
    - I called him to help, and he agreed immediately.
  - 医(醫)生( )叫( )我( )每( )天( )多( )喝( )水( )。
    - Yīshēng jiào wǒ měitiān duō hē shuǐ.
    - The doctor told me to drink more water every day.
- **historical forms:**

### 叫 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)

- **definition:** hook
- **pinyin:** jiū
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two entangled ropes ->
    - to entangle; to intertwine
  - **interpretation:** The character 丩 (jiū, "twist") depicts two ropes twisted together, symbolizing the concept of entangling or intertwining.

- **pinyin:** huǒ

  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火( )在( )壁( )炉(爐)中( )熊( )熊( )燃( )烧(燒)。

    - Yěwài lùyíng shí, huǒ néng qūzǒu hánlěng.
    - When camping outdoors, the fire can drive away the cold.
  - 遇( )到( )火( )灾(災)时(時)，迅( )速( )疏( )散( )最( )为(為)重( )要( )。
    - Yù dào huǒzāi shí, xùnsù shū sàn zuìwéi zhòngyào.
    - In case of a fire, evacuating quickly is of utmost importance.

## 灭(滅)
---
## (of a light, fire, etc.) go out
### miè
---
- **traditional:** 滅
- **definition:** (of a light, fire, etc.) go out
- **pinyin:** miè
- **components:**
  - 氵(水)
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 烕
    - huǐ
    - extinguish, destroy
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 氵(水, 'water') + 烕(烕, phonetic) =
    - to destroy with water ->
    - extinguish
  - **interpretation:** The character 滅 combines the water radical 氵(水, 'water') and the phonetic 烕, symbolizing the extinguishing of a fire or destruction by flooding. This reflects the imagery of using water to put out or destroy something.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 滅 was simplified to 灭(滅) by removing the components 氵(水, 'water') and 戊(戊, 'fifth heavenly stem') while retaining the core phonetic and semantic composition.
- **examples:**
  - 火( )焰( )熄( )灭(滅)了( )。
    - Huǒyàn xīmiè le.
    - The flame went out.
  - 灯(燈)光( )在( )暴( )风(風)雨( )中( )熄( )灭(滅)，我( )们(們)陷( )入( )黑( )暗( )。
    - Dēngguāng zài bàofēngyǔ zhōng xīmiè，wǒmen xiànrù hēi'àn.
    - The lights went out during the storm, and we fell into darkness.
  - 他( )的( )希( )望( )已( )经(經)破( )灭(滅)。
    - Tā de xīwàng yǐjīng pòmiè.
    - His hopes have already been shattered.
### 灭(滅) → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字( )中( )偏( )旁( )氵( )，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快( )戏(戲)水( )。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 灭(滅) → 烕
- **definition:** extinguish, destroy
- **pinyin:** huǐ
- **components:**
  - 戌
    - xū
    - ninth month
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 戌 + semantic 火 (fire) ->
    - extinguish
  - **interpretation:** The character 烕 (huǐ, "extinguish, destroy") combines the phonetic component 戌 (xū, "ninth month") with the semantic component 火 (huǒ, "fire"). The phonetic component contributes the sound, while the fire component indicates the meaning related to fire. The overall sense of extinguishing or destroying suggests the extinguishing of a fire.
### 灭(滅) → 烕 → 戌
- **definition:** ninth month
- **pinyin:** xū
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant
  - **description:**
    - Originally variant form of 恤 ->
    - related to 裇
  - **interpretation:** The character 戌 was originally a variant of 恤, which is connected to 裇 in etymology. Both characters relate to phono-semantic compounds involving 衤 with
- **historical forms:**

## 讨(討)厌(厭)
---
## dislike
### tǎoyàn
---
- **traditional:** 討厭
- **definition:** dislike
- **pinyin:** tǎoyàn
- **components:**
  - 讨(討)
    - tǎo
    - demand; discuss; ask for
  - 厌(厭)
    - yàn
    - aversion; detest; be fed up with; be tired of
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 討 (tǎo, "demand") and 厭 (yàn, "aversion") together convey developing a feeling of aversion in response to a demand or bother, leading to 'dislike' or 'annoyance'.
  - **interpretation:** 討 (tǎo, "demand") represents the idea of demands or engagements, often leading to irritation. 厭 (yàn, "aversion") captures the feeling of detachment or weariness that can result from such demands. Together, they imply a state where ongoing demands lead to annoyance or dislike, forming the idea of 'dislike'. This reflects the emotional response to feeling burdened or overwhelmed by unwanted interactions.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )讨(討)厌(厭)吃( )辣( )的( )食( )物( )。
    - Wǒ tǎoyàn chī là de shíwù.
    - I dislike eating spicy food.
  - 他( )总(總)是( )迟(遲)到( )，真( )让(讓)人( )讨(討)厌(厭)。
    - Tā zǒng shì chídào, zhēn ràng rén tǎoyàn.
    - He's always late, which is really annoying.
  - 这(這)个(個)天( )气(氣)让(讓)我( )很( )讨(討)厌(厭)。
    - Zhège tiānqì ràng wǒ hěn tǎoyàn.
    - This weather makes me very annoyed.
### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 讨(討)
- **traditional:** 討
- **definition:** demand; discuss; ask for
- **pinyin:** tǎo
- **components:**
  - 言
    - yán
    - speech
  - 肘
    - zhǒu
    - elbow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 言 (yán, "speech") + phonetic 肘 ->
    - speech-initiated action
  - **interpretation:** 言 (yán, "speech") indicates the involvement of speaking or communication, while 肘 provides the phonetic element. The concept is of a speech-initiated action, like asking or demanding something by speaking. The action element hints at intention, bridging to meanings like 'ask for' or 'demand'.
  - **simplification:** In the simplification to 讨, 言 (yán, "speech") was replaced by its simplified form 讠, reducing the number of strokes while retaining the phonetic element.
- **examples:**
  - 孩( )子( )们(們)总(總)是( )讨(討)糖( )果( )。
    - Háizimen zǒng shì tǎo tángguǒ.
    - The children always beg for candy.
  - 他( )讨(討)工( )资(資)时(時)，老( )板(闆)总(總)推( )脱(脫)。
    - Tā tǎo gōngzī shí, lǎobǎn zǒng tuītuō.
    - When he asks for his salary, the boss always evades.
  - 你( )能( )不( )能( )替( )我( )讨(討)一( )个(個)公( )道( )？
    - Nǐ néng bù néng tì wǒ tǎo yī gè gōngdào?
    - Can you help me demand justice?
### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 讨(討) → 言
- **definition:** speech
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 舌
    - shé
    - tongue
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 舌 (mouth with a forked tongue) with added stroke at top to suggest tongue movement ->
    - speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 言(yán, "speech") depicts the addition of a horizontal stroke to the ancient form of 舌(shé, "tongue") to indicate the motion of the tongue as it moves to articulate speech. This directly connects the organ involved in speaking to the concept of speech itself.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )言( )语(語)充( )满(滿)智( )慧( )。
    - Tā de yányǔ chōngmǎn zhìhuì.
    - His speech is full of wisdom.
  - 我( )们(們)应(應)该(該)以( )行( )动(動)证(證)明( )我( )们(們)的( )言( )词(詞)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi yǐ xíngdòng zhèngmíng wǒmen de yáncí.
    - We should prove our words with actions.
  - 他( )说(說)话(話)的( )方( )式( )显(顯)示( )了( )他( )的( )修( )养(養)。
    - Tā shuōhuà de fāngshì xiǎnshìle tā de xiūyǎng.
    - The way he speaks shows his refinement.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 言](@media/glyph8a00.png)
### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 讨(討) → 言 → 舌
- **definition:** tongue
- **pinyin:** shé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a forked tongue emerging upwards from a mouth
  - **interpretation:** The character 舌(shé, 'tongue') visually represents a tongue extending out from a mouth, which aligns with its meaning. This direct depiction makes it easy to remember its association with speech and taste in its semantic family, also relating to words like 言(yán, 'word').
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )舌( )非( )常( )灵(靈)敏( )。
    - Tā de shé fēicháng língmǐn.
    - His tongue is very sensitive.
  - 品( )尝(嚐)美( )食( )时(時)，他( )的( )舌( )细(細)品( )滋( )味( )。
    - Pǐncháng měishí shí, tā de shé xì pǐn zīwèi.
    - While tasting delicious food, his tongue savors every flavor.
  - 他( )长(長)舌( )无(無)忌( )，经(經)常( )泄( )露( )秘( )密( )。
    - Tā chángshé wújì, jīngcháng xièlòu mìmì.
    - He is talkative and often spills secrets.

### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 讨(討) → 言 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.

    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.

### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 讨(討) → 肘
- **definition:** elbow
- **pinyin:** zhǒu
- **components:**
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
  - 肉
    - ròu
    - meat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 寸 (hand indicating measurement) with 肉 (meat/flesh) added for distinction ->
    - 肘
  - **interpretation:** The character 肘 (zhǒu, "elbow") combines 寸 (cùn, "inch"), originally depicting a hand with a stroke for the elbow, with 肉 (ròu, "meat") to specifically indicate the fleshiness of the elbow area in the human body.
- **examples:**
  - 他撞到了我的肘。
    - Tā zhuàng dào le wǒ de zhǒu.
    - He bumped into my elbow.
  - 在( )瑜( )伽( )课(課)上( )，我们学习如何将肘贴(貼)地( )。
    - Zài yújiākè shàng, wǒmen xuéxí rúhé jiāng zhǒu tiē dì.
    - In yoga class, we learn how to place our elbows on the ground.
  - 医(醫)生( )建( )议(議)我( )，在( )锻(鍛)炼(鍊)时(時)保护好肘( )关(關)节(節)。
    - Yīshēng jiànyì wǒ, zài duànliàn shí bǎohù hǎo zhǒu guānjié.
    - The doctor advised me to protect my elbow joint during exercise.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 肘](@media/glyph8098.png)
### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 讨(討) → 肘 → 寸
- **definition:** inch
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)块(塊)布( )每( )一( )寸( )都( )是( )精( )心( )制(製)作( )。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用( )卷( )尺( )量( )一( )寸( )，每( )一( )寸( )数(數)据(據)都( )准(準)确(確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寸](@media/glyph5bf8.png)
### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 讨(討) → 肘 → 肉
- **definition:** meat
- **pinyin:** ròu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a piece of flesh or meat with stripes representing texture.
  - **interpretation:** The character 肉(ròu, "flesh") depicts a piece of meat, meant to evoke the concept of flesh through its visual resemblance to a striped or sectioned piece of meat.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )喜( )欢(歡)吃( )肉( )。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī ròu.
    - I like eating meat.
  - 这(這)块(塊)肉( )很( )鲜(鮮)美( )，营(營)养(養)丰(豐)富( )。

### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 厌(厭)
- **traditional:** 厭
- **definition:** aversion; detest; be fed up with; be tired of
- **pinyin:** yàn
- **components:**
  - 厂
    - chǎng
    - cliff
  - 猒
    - yàn
    - abundant; excessive
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 厂 (chǎng, "cliff") + phonetic 猒 (yàn) ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** In 厭 (yàn, "to loathe; bore; disgust"), the semantic component 厂 (chǎng, "cliff") conveys an image of something oppressive or imposing, while the phonetic component 猒 (yàn), which carries a similar sound, helps to form the character's pronunciation. This combination suggests the overwhelming nature of loathing or disgust, as if something metaphorically looms over a person like a cliff.
  - **simplification:** The character 厭 was simplified to 厌 by removing the phonetic component 猒 (yàn), keeping the meaning while reducing strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )对(對)重( )复(複)的( )工( )作( )感( )到( )厌(厭)倦( )。
    - Tā duì chóngfù de gōngzuò gǎndào yànjuàn.
    - He feels weary of the repetitive work.
  - 过(過)于(於)复(複)杂(雜)的( )程( )序( )让(讓)人( )厌(厭)烦(煩)。
    - Guòyú fùzá de chéngxù ràng rén yànfán.
    - The overly complicated procedure is annoying.
  - 她( )对(對)快( )餐( )感( )到( )厌(厭)恶(惡)。
    - Tā duì kuàicān gǎndào yànwù.
    - She feels disgusted with fast food.

  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**

    - factory
  - **interpretation:** The character 廠 (chǎng, "factory") combines the semantic element 广 (guǎng, "shelter") with the phonetic element 敞 (chǎng, "open; spacious"), suggesting a large, open building used for production, akin to a factory.
  - **simplification:** 厂 is a simplified form by removing the phonetic component 敞 while retaining the basic shelter concept from 广, streamlining it to represent 'cliff' or 'factory'.

- **definition:** broad
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 广
    - guǎng
    - roof; shelter
  - 黃
    - huáng
    - yellow

  - **description:**
    - semantic 广 (roof; shelter) + phonetic 黃 (huáng, sound) ->
    - shelter
  - **interpretation:** The character 廣 (guǎng, 'shelter') combines the semantic component 广, which suggests the idea of covering or enclosure like a roof, with the phonetic component 黃 (huáng). The enclosure aspect of 广 underlines the meaning of providing shelter or an expansive space.

### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 厌(厭) → 厂(廠) → 广(廣) → 廣 → 黃
- **definition:** yellow
- **pinyin:** huáng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally a pictogram depicting a disabled person or man with a ring of jade on the chest ->
    - phonetically borrowed for 'yellow' ->
    - 黃
  - **interpretation:** The character 黃 (huáng, 'yellow') originated from a pictogram representing either a disabled person or a man with a jade ring, showing a connection to cultural rituals or symbols of status. It was later phonetically borrowed to represent the color 'yellow' without semantic connection to its original depiction. In modern Chinese, its primary use is to denote the color yellow, disconnecting entirely from its debated pictographic origins.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)朵( )花( )是( )黄(黃)色( )的( )。
    - Zhè duǒ huā shì huángsè de.
    - This flower is yellow.
  - 秋( )天( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，树(樹)叶(葉)变(變)成( )金( )黄(黃)色( )。
    - Qiūtiān láilín shí, shùyè biàn chéng jīnhuáng sè.
    - When autumn arrives, the leaves turn golden yellow.

    - Tā chuānle yī jiàn huángsè de wàitào.
    - He wore a yellow jacket.

### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 厌(厭) → 厂(廠) → 敞 → 尚 → 向
- **definition:** face; towards
- **pinyin:** xiàng
- **components:**
  - 宀
    - mián
    - house
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 宀 (house) + 口 (mouth) =
    - echos in a place ->
    - original form of 響
  - **interpretation:** The character 向 (xiàng, 'towards') originally depicted echoes in a space, suggesting a sound emanating within a house. Over time, this visual evolved into denoting a direction or orientation, similar to how a sound moves towards something. Thus, it was used to express the concept of 'towards.'

    - Tā xiàng wǒ wēixiào.
    - She smiled towards me.

### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 厌(厭) → 猒
- **definition:** abundant; excessive
- **pinyin:** yàn
- **components:**
  - 犬
    - quǎn
    - dog
  - 甘
    - gān
    - sweet
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - ⺼
    - ròu
    - meat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 犬 (dog) + 口 (mouth, corrupted to 甘 and later 日) + ⺼ (meat) ->
    - a dog eating meat ->
    - satisfied
  - **interpretation:** The character 猒 originally depicted a dog 犬 (quǎn, 'dog') eating from a mouth 口 (kǒu, 'mouth') filled with meat ⺼ (ròu, 'meat'), illustrating a state of being 'satisfied' after consuming a meal. Over time, the component 口 transformed into 甘 (gān, 'sweet') and then 日 (rì, 'sun'), keeping the basic imagery of fulfillment or satisfaction intact. This concept also extends to a feeling of weariness that often follows complete satisfaction.

### 讨(討)厌(厭) → 厌(厭) → 猒 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨( )曦( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日( )出( )东(東)方( )。

    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中( )午( )时(時)分( )，日( )高( )挂(掛)天( )。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.

## 小( )声(聲)
---
## in a low voice
### xiǎoshēng
---
- **traditional:** 小聲
- **definition:** in a low voice
- **pinyin:** xiǎoshēng
- **components:**
  - 小
    - xiǎo
    - small; few
  - 声(聲)
    - shēng
    - sound; voice
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 小 (xiǎo, "small; few") refers to something small or in a reduced form. 聲 (shēng, "sound; voice") refers to sound or voice. Together, 小聲 refers to speaking or making sounds in a low, soft manner.
  - **interpretation:** 小( )聲(声) (xiǎoshēng, "in a low voice") literally means 'small voice', suggesting speaking quietly or softly, which is often used to describe speaking in a whisper or to avoid being overheard.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )小( )声(聲)地( )说(說)，怕吵醒孩子。
    - Tā xiǎoshēng de shuō, pà chǎoxǐng háizi.
    - She spoke in a low voice, afraid of waking the child.
  - 请(請)小( )声(聲)一( )点(點)，以( )免( )影( )响(響)别(別)人( )。
    - Qǐng xiǎoshēng yīdiǎn, yǐmiǎn yǐngxiǎng biérén.
    - Please speak a little softer to avoid disturbing others.
  - 他( )常( )常( )小( )声(聲)地( )唱( )歌( )。
    - Tā chángcháng xiǎoshēng de chànggē.
    - He often sings in a low voice.
### 小( )声(聲) → 小
- **definition:** small; few
- **pinyin:** xiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts three small dots arranged symmetrically to represent something small
  - **interpretation:** The character 小(xiǎo, 'small') uses three small strokes to symbolize size or quantity, visually capturing the essence of 'smallness'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小( )猫(貓)很( )可( )爱(愛)。
    - Zhège xiǎo māo hěn kě'ài.
    - This small cat is very cute.
  - 这(這)座( )小( )桥(橋)横(橫)跨( )河( )流( )，连(連)接( )两(兩)岸( )。
    - Zhè zuò xiǎo qiáo héngkuà héliú, liánjiē liǎng àn.
    - This small bridge spans the river, connecting both banks.
  - 请(請)给(給)我( )一( )小( )杯( )水( )。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ yī xiǎo bēi shuǐ.
    - Please give me a small cup of water.

### 小( )声(聲) → 声(聲)
- **traditional:** 聲
- **definition:** sound; voice
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 耳
    - ěr
    - ear
  - 殸
    - qìng
    - an ancient chime stone
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 耳 (ěr, "ear") + phonetic 殸 ->
    - perception of sounds
  - **interpretation:** The character 聲 (shēng, "sound"; "voice") combines 耳 (ěr, "ear") as the semantic component, suggesting listening or hearing, with 殸 as the phonetic component, to produce the concept of a sound as perceived by the ear.
  - **simplification:** 声 is a simplified form where the character 殸 has been reduced to 士 (shì, "scholar") plus the addition of 𠂇 (movement), dropping the 耳 (ěr, "ear") component for simplicity.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )听(聽)到( )了( )一( )种(種)奇( )怪( )的( )声(聲)音( )。
    - Wǒ tīngdào le yī zhǒng qíguài de shēngyīn.
    - I heard a strange sound.
  - 鸟(鳥)儿(兒)在( )树(樹)上( )快( )乐(樂)地( )歌( )唱( )，它( )们(們)的( )声(聲)音( )如( )音( )乐(樂)般( )动(動)听(聽)。
    - Niǎor men zài shù shàng kuàilè de gēchàng, tāmen de shēngyīn rú yīnyuè bān dòngtīng.
    - The birds sing happily on the tree, and their voices are as melodious as music.
  - 老( )师(師)的( )声(聲)音( )充( )满(滿)了( )自( )信( )，让(讓)学(學)生( )们(們)感( )受( )到( )安( )全( )。
    - Lǎoshī de shēngyīn chōngmǎnle zìxìn, ràng xuéshēngmen gǎnshòudào ānquán.
    - The teacher's voice was full of confidence, making the students feel safe.
### 小( )声(聲) → 声(聲) → 耳
- **definition:** ear
- **pinyin:** ěr
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an ear
  - **interpretation:** The character 耳 (ěr, "ear") is a pictogram that visually represents an ear with its distinctive shape. This straightforward representation made it intuitive for ancient speakers to associate the character directly with the concept of an ear.
- **examples:**
  - 音( )乐(樂)直( )入( )耳( )。
    - Yīn yuè zhí rù ěr.
    - The music goes straight to the ear.

    - a stone chime being struck by a mallet ->
    - vessel; sound
  - **interpretation:** The character 殸(kēng, "vessel; sound") visually represents a hand wielding a mallet striking a stone chime, signifying the action of creating sound or the vessel on which it is made. This composition intentionally evokes the sounds produced by striking.

## 巴掌

## palm; slap
### bāzhang
---
- **definition:** palm; slap
- **pinyin:** bāzhang
- **components:**
  - 巴
    - bā
    - to hold onto; cling
  - 掌
    - zhǎng
    - palm; to slap
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 巴(bā, "to hold onto; cling") 掌(zhǎng, "palm; to slap")
  - **interpretation:** 巴(bā, "to hold onto; cling to") suggests grasping onto something, which links to the idea of a 'palm' where one holds or grasps items. 掌(zhǎng, "palm; to slap") directly describes the flat, broad shape of the hand's palm, fitting its role in slapping. Together, 巴掌(bāzhang) conveys the sense of a palm, a part of the hand capable of clinging and slapping.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )愤(憤)怒( )地( )拍( )了( )一( )下( )巴( )掌( )。
    - Tā fènnù de pāile yīxià bāzhang.
    - He angrily slapped his palm.
  - 孩( )子( )用( )力( )地( )击(擊)了( )一( )下( )自( )己( )的( )巴( )掌( )。
    - Háizi yònglì de jīle yīxià zìjǐ de bāzhang.
    - The child forcefully slapped his own palm.
  - 他( )的( )巴( )掌( )打( )得( )很( )响(響)。
    - Tā de bāzhang dǎ de hěn xiǎng.
    - His slap was very loud.
### 巴掌 → 巴
- **definition:** to hold onto; cling
- **pinyin:** bā
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a huge snake
  - **interpretation:** The character 巴(bā, "to cling") originally depicted a large snake. The image of a snake conveys the idea of clinging or sticking closely to something, which connects to the primary meaning of the character. Additionally, it can metaphorically represent a surname, possibly due to historical or cultural associations.
- **examples:**
  - 小( )狗( )紧(緊)紧(緊)地( )巴( )在( )妈(媽)妈(媽)的( )身( )边(邊)。
    - Xiǎo gǒu jǐn jǐn de bā zài māma de shēnbiān.
    - The puppy clings tightly to the mother's side.
  - 巴( )叔( )叔( )是( )个(個)很( )友( )好( )的( )人( )。
    - Bā shūshu shì gè hěn yǒuhǎo de rén.
    - Uncle Ba is a very friendly person.
  - 孩( )子( )们(們)手( )里(裡)拿( )着( )糖( )果( )，巴( )巴( )地( )看( )着( )我( )们(們)。
    - Háizimen shǒu lǐ názhe tángguǒ, bābā de kànzhe wǒmen.
    - The children were holding candies and looking at us eagerly.

### 巴掌 → 掌

    - shàng
    - esteem
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 尚 (shàng, "esteem") as phonetic + 手 (shǒu, "hand") as semantic =
    - related to the hand ->
    - palm, control
  - **interpretation:** The character 掌 combines the phonetic component 尚 (shàng, "esteem") with the semantic component 手 (shǒu, "hand") to indicate its meaning related to the hand, specifically the palm, which is often associated with handling or controlling something.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )的( )手( )掌( )很( )宽(寬)大( )。
    - Tā de shǒuzhǎng hěn kuāndà.

### 巴掌 → 掌 → 尚
- **definition:** esteem
- **pinyin:** shàng
- **components:**
  - 八
    - bā
    - eight
  - 向
    - xiàng
    - face; towards
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 八 (bā, "eight") + phonetic 向 (xiàng, "face; towards") ->
    - meaning
  - **interpretation:** The character 尚(shàng, "esteem") combines 八 (bā, "eight"), which acts as the semantic component, with 向 (xiàng, "face; towards"), which provides the phonetic sound. The sense of moving towards something in 向 supports ideas of ascending or elevating, hence developing into the sense of 'esteem' associated with elevating status or regard.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )作( )风(風)很( )时(時)尚( )。

    - Tā zǒng shì zhuīqiú gāoshàng de lǐxiǎng.
    - She always pursues noble ideals.
  - 他( )是( )一( )个(個)很( )有( )思( )想( )的( )人( )，大家都很敬仰他。
    - Tā shì yīgè hěn yǒu sīxiǎng de rén, dàjiā dōu hěn jìngyǎng tā.
    - He is a person with great ideas, and everyone esteems him.

### 巴掌 → 掌 → 尚 → 向
- **definition:** face; towards
- **pinyin:** xiàng
- **components:**
  - 宀
    - mián
    - house
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 宀 (house) + 口 (mouth) =
    - echos in a place ->
    - original form of 響
  - **interpretation:** The character 向 (xiàng, 'towards') originally depicted echoes in a space, suggesting a sound emanating within a house. Over time, this visual evolved into denoting a direction or orientation, similar to how a sound moves towards something. Thus, it was used to express the concept of 'towards.'
- **examples:**
  - 她向我微笑。
    - Tā xiàng wǒ wēixiào.
    - She smiled towards me.
  - 船( )正( )向( )港( )口( )驶(駛)去( )。
    - Chuán zhèng xiàng gǎngkǒu shǐqù.
    - The ship is sailing towards the port.

    - Tā xiàng lǎoshī qǐngjiào wèntí.

### 巴掌 → 掌 → 尚 → 向 → 宀
- **definition:** house
- **pinyin:** mián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a house with four walls ->
    - roof
  - **interpretation:** 宀(mián, "roof") is a pictogram representing a house with four walls. It emphasizes an enclosed space, distinguishing it from similar structures like 广(guǎng, "broad") which depicts a building with three walls. This makes 宀 a logical choice for representing a roof in various characters.
- **examples:**
  - 含( )有( )宀( )的( )汉(漢)字( )代( )表( )家( )的( )温(溫)暖( )。
    - Hán yǒu mián de hànzì dàibiǎo jiā de wēnnuǎn.
    - Chinese characters that include the radical '宀' represent the warmth of home.
  - 屋( )顶(頂)遮( )风(風)挡(擋)雨( )，家( )园(園)散( )发(發)温(溫)馨( )。
    - Wūdǐng zhē fēng dǎng yǔ, jiāyuán sànfā wēnxīn.
    - The roof shields from wind and rain, and the home radiates warmth.

### 巴掌 → 掌 → 尚 → 向 → 口

- **pinyin:** kǒu

  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。

    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.

  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.

## 一( )辈(輩)子( )
---
## all one's life; throughout one's life
### yíbèizi
---
- **traditional:** 一輩子
- **definition:** all one's life; throughout one's life
- **pinyin:** yíbèizi
- **components:**
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 辈(輩)
    - bèi
    - generation; lifetime; contemporaries
  - 子
    - zi
    - noun suffix; son; child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 一 (yī, "one") + 辈(輩) (bèi, "generation") + 子 (zi, "noun suffix")
  - **interpretation:** The term 一輩子 (yíbèizi) literally translates to 'one generation', with the addition of the suffix 子 (zi, "noun suffix") to denote a duration of time encompassing one's entire lifetime, emphasizing continuity and entirety.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )想( )一( )辈(輩)子( )守( )护(護)你( )。
    - Wǒ xiǎng yíbèizi shǒuhù nǐ.
    - I want to protect you all my life.
  - 他( )一( )辈(輩)子( )都( )在( )追( )求( )真( )理( )。
    - Tā yíbèizi dōu zài zhuīqiú zhēnlǐ.
    - He has been pursuing the truth all his life.
  - 一( )辈(輩)子( )生( )活( )在( )这(這)个(個)小( )镇(鎮)上( )，他( )已( )经(經)和( )这(這)里(裡)融( )为(為)一( )体(體)。
    - Yíbèizi shēnghuó zài zhège xiǎo zhèn shàng, tā yǐjīng hé zhèlǐ róng wéi yī tǐ.
    - Having lived in this small town all his life, he has become one with it.
### 一( )辈(輩)子( ) → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )一( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他( )只( )看( )到( )一( )只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了( )花( )园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一( )条(條)直( )路( )通( )向( )远(遠)方( )。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 一](@media/glyph4e00.png)
### 一( )辈(輩)子( ) → 辈(輩)
- **traditional:** 輩
- **definition:** generation; lifetime; contemporaries
- **pinyin:** bèi
- **components:**
  - 車
    - chē
    - cart
  - 非
    - fēi
    - not
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 車 (chē, "cart") + phonetic 非 (fēi) ->
    - generation
  - **interpretation:** The character 輩 combines the semantic 車 (chē, "cart") with the phonetic 非 (fēi) to denote the idea of generation. While 車 suggests movement or procession, a sense connected to sequential progression or the passage of time, 非 provides the phonetic element. The notion of a series of carts can metaphorically relate to successive generations, each following the one before, forming the concept of 'generation' or 'lifetime.'
  - **simplification:** 輩 was simplified to 辈(輩) by reducing 車 to the simpler form of 车 while retaining the phonetic 非 (fēi).
- **examples:**
  - 年( )轻(輕)一( )代( )正( )引( )领(領)科( )技( )创(創)新( )。
    - Niánqīng yī dài zhèng yǐnlǐng kējì chuàngxīn.
    - The younger generation is leading technological innovation.
  - 他( )一( )生( )致( )力( )于(於)教( )育( )事( )业(業)。
    - Tā yīshēng zhìlì yú jiàoyù shìyè.
    - He dedicated his lifetime to the cause of education.
  - 祖( )辈(輩)的智慧对(對)我( )们(們)影( )响(響)深( )远(遠)。
    - Zǔbèi de zhìhuì duì wǒmen yǐngxiǎng shēnyuǎn.
    - The wisdom of the ancestors has a profound influence on us.
### 一( )辈(輩)子( ) → 辈(輩) → 車
- **definition:** cart
- **pinyin:** chē
- **components:**
  - 田
    - tián
    - field
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a carriage viewed from above; wheels on both sides + sun shade on top ->
    - depicted vertically with wheels as strokes and loading area marked by 田 (tián, "field") ->
    - 車
  - **interpretation:** The character 車(chē, "vehicle") originally depicts a carriage from an overhead perspective. The transformation into the vertical form involved simplifying the depiction of wheels and emphasizing the loading area, marked by a field symbol, creating a streamlined pictographic representation.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 車 was simplified to 车 by reducing the number of strokes, maintaining the overall shape of the vehicle but removing intricate details.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )坐( )车(車)去( )上( )班( )。
    - Wǒ zuò chē qù shàngbān.
    - I take a car to go to work.
  - 这(這)辆(輛)车(車)很( )快( )。
    - Zhè liàng chē hěn kuài.
    - This car is very fast.
  - 我( )想( )买(買)一( )辆(輛)新( )车(車)。
    - Wǒ xiǎng mǎi yī liàng xīn chē.
    - I want to buy a new car.
- **historical forms:**

  - **interpretation:** The character 非 (fēi, "not") visually resembles two wings turned away from each other, symbolizing opposition and disagreement. This imagery captures the essence of negation, which is central to the character's meaning.

### 一( )辈(輩)子( ) → 子

  - **interpretation:** The character 子(zǐ, "child") is a pictorial representation of a baby, emphasizing characteristics like a large head and outstretched arms typical of infants, which conveys the essence of a child. This visual element helps infer its meaning.

## 得
---
## get; obtain; win
### dé
---
- **definition:** get; obtain; win
- **pinyin:** dé
- **components:**
  - 貝
    - bèi
    - cowry
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 彳
    - chì
    - step
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
  - 旦
    - dàn
    - dawn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 貝 (bèi, 'cowry') + 又 (yòu, 'hand') ->
    - obtaining valuables ->
    - 彳 (chì, 'step') added, 又 changed to 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), 貝 corrupted to 旦 (dàn, 'dawn') ->
    - final form
  - **interpretation:** The character originated as a depiction of a hand picking up a cowry, symbolizing 'obtaining' valuables. The 彳 (chì, 'step') was added to suggest movement on a road, enhancing the idea of acquisition. Over time, script evolutions saw substitute elements: the component 又 (yòu, 'hand') changed to 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), reflecting the Qin script's tendency, and 貝 (bèi, 'cowry') was simplified to 旦 (dàn, 'dawn'). These changes led to the character's modern form. This transition mirrors the evolved meanings in usage: 'to get', from obtaining something physically; 'must', representing the necessity of movement or action; and its role as a structural particle in grammar for completion or necessity in expressions.
  - **simplification:** In simplified form, 得 remains unchanged from its traditional representation.
- **examples:**
  - 他跑得很快。
    - Tā pǎo de hěn kuài.
    - He runs very fast.
  - 我得去工作。
    - Wǒ děi qù gōngzuò.
    - I have to go to work.
  - 她( )昨( )天( )赢(贏)得( )了( )比( )赛(賽)。
    - Tā zuótiān yíngdé le bǐsài.
    - She won the competition yesterday.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 得](@media/glyph5f97.png)
### 得 → 貝
- **definition:** cowry
- **pinyin:** bèi
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a cowrie shell ->
    - used as currency in ancient China ->
    - stylized as 貝
  - **interpretation:** The character 貝(bèi, 'shell/money') visually represents a cowrie shell, which was used as a form of currency in ancient China. This explains why it is associated with money or valuables.
  - **simplification:** 贝 is a cursive script simplification of 貝, transforming the character into a more streamlined form while retaining its essence.
- **examples:**
  - 他把贝(貝)当作护(護)身( )符( )，放在口( )袋( )里(裡)。
    - Tā bǎ bèi dāng zuò hùshēn fú, fàng zài kǒudài lǐ.
    - He uses shells as a talisman, placing them in his pocket.
  - 古( )代( )人( )用( )贝(貝)作( )为(為)货(貨)币(幣)。
    - Gǔdài rén yòng bèi zuòwéi huòbì.
    - In ancient times, people used shells as currency.
### 得 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又( )」这(這)个(個)字( )最( )早( )来(來)源( )于(於)手( )。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很( )多( )汉(漢)字( )含( )有( )又( )部( )首( )，表( )示( )与(與)手( )有( )关(關)的( )动(動)作( )。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古( )人( )用( )又( )描( )绘(繪)手( )的( )形( )态(態)，体(體)现(現)了( )古( )汉(漢)字( )的( )独(獨)特( )魅( )力( )。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 又](@media/glyph53c8.png)
### 得 → 彳
- **definition:** step
- **pinyin:** chì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a foot or person walking
  - **interpretation:** 彳(chì, 'walking') visually represents steps or a person moving, suggesting the idea of walking or movement. Despite a simplified history from characters like 行(xíng, 'walk'), its pictographic heritage directly connects with the notion of stepping or proceeding.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )喜( )欢(歡)在( )河( )边(邊)慢( )慢( )地( )走( )。
    - Tā xǐhuān zài hé biān mànmàn de zǒu.
    - He likes to walk slowly by the river.
  - 我( )们(們)每( )天( )退( )出( )喧( )嚣(囂)，享( )受( )安( )静(靜)的( )散( )步( )。
    - Wǒmen měitiān tuìchū xuānxiāo, xiǎngshòu ānjìng de sànbù.
    - We withdraw from the hustle and bustle every day to enjoy a quiet walk.
  - 他( )常( )常( )独(獨)自( )彳( )亍( )于(於)公( )园(園)小( )径(徑)。
    - Tā chángcháng dúzì chìchù yú gōngyuán xiǎojìng.
    - He often walks alone on the park trails.

![Historical forms of 彳](@media/glyph5f73.png)
### 得 → 寸
- **definition:** inch
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)块(塊)布( )每( )一( )寸( )都( )是( )精( )心( )制(製)作( )。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用( )卷( )尺( )量( )一( )寸( )，每( )一( )寸( )数(數)据(據)都( )准(準)确(確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
- **historical forms:**

### 得 → 旦
- **definition:** dawn
- **pinyin:** dàn
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 丁
    - dīng
    - nail
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, "sun") + 丁 (dīng, "nail") =
    - sun appearing over the horizon, 丁 indicates pronunciation
  - **interpretation:** Although the original interpretation is debated, the character combines 日 (rì, "sun") and 丁 (dīng, "nail") to depict the sun rising. This is a visual representation of dawn, where the sun emerges at the horizon line.
- **examples:**
  - 破( )晓(曉)的( )旦( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)山( )川( )。
    - Pòxiǎo de dàn guāng sǎ mǎn shānchuān.
    - The light of dawn scattered over the mountains and rivers.
  - 黎( )明( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，旦( )光( )映( )红(紅)天( )边(邊)。
    - Límíng láilín shí, dàn guāng yìng hóng tiānbiān.
    - When dawn arrives, the light of dawn paints the sky red.
  - 在( )寂( )静(靜)的( )山( )谷( )中( )，天( )边(邊)的( )旦( )光( )预(預)告( )着(著)新( )生( )。
    - Zài jìjìng de shāngǔ zhōng, tiānbiān de dàn guāng yùgào zhe xīnshēng.
    - In the quiet valley, the light of dawn heralds new life.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 旦](@media/glyph65e6.png)
### 得 → 旦 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨( )曦( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日( )出( )东(東)方( )。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖( )的( )日( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中( )午( )时(時)分( )，日( )高( )挂(掛)天( )。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 得 → 旦 → 丁
- **definition:** nail
- **pinyin:** dīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of a nail ->
    - 丁
  - **interpretation:** The character 丁 originally depicted the head of a nail, emphasizing simplicity and directness. While it has developed other interpretations over time, such as a head or city wall, these relate to similar shapes and functions. Today, 釘 (dīng, 'nail') reflects this meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 工( )人( )熟( )练(練)地( )把( )丁( )敲( )进(進)了( )墙(牆)壁( )。
    - Gōngrén shúliàn de bǎ dīng qiāng jìnle qiángbì.
    - The worker skillfully hammered the nail into the wall.
  - 他( )精( )心( )挑( )选(選)了( )铁(鐵)质(質)丁( )，确(確)保( )家(傢)具(俱)稳(穩)固( )。
    - Tā jīngxīn tiāoxuǎnle tiě zhì dīng, quèbǎo jiājù wěngù.
    - He carefully selected the iron nail to ensure the furniture was stable.
  - 请(請)把( )散( )落( )的( )丁( )收( )好( )。
    - Qǐng bǎ sànluò de dīng shōuhǎo.
    - Please gather the scattered nails.

## 了
---
## used after a verb with 得/不 to express possibility or impossibility
### liǎo
---
- **definition:** used after a verb with 得/不 to express possibility or impossibility
- **pinyin:** liǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a baby without arms (compare 子 with arms) ->
    - entangled legs ->
    - sound loan for 'finish'
  - **interpretation:** The original depiction is of a baby shape illustrating a state of vulnerability or incompleteness. Over time, the idea of 'entangled legs' metaphorically transitioned into 'something tied or completed.' 'Finish' likely arose from a sound loan rather than semantic combination, as 'entangled' implies coming to an end or conclusion in a motion.
- **examples:**
  - 事( )情( )已( )经(經)结(結)束( )了( )。
    - Shìqíng yǐjīng jiéshù le.
    - The matter has already ended.
  - 他( )终(終)于(於)明( )白( )了( )。
    - Tā zhōngyú míngbái le.
    - He finally understood.
  - 她( )在( )一( )小( )时(時)内(內)完( )成( )了( )这(這)项(項)任( )务(務)。
    - Tā zài yī xiǎoshí nèi wánchéng le zhè xiàng rènwù.
    - She completed this task within an hour.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 了](@media/glyph4e86.png)

## 了
### liǎo

## used after a verb with 得/不 to express possibility or impossibility

## 敢
---
## dare
### gǎn
---
- **definition:** dare
- **pinyin:** gǎn
- **components:**
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 豕
    - shǐ
    - boar
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 又 (yòu, 'hand') + 豕 (shǐ, 'boar') with capturing tool 𰅱 ->
    - hand using tool to hunt boar ->
    - 𰅱 omitted, 口/甘 added redudantly ->
    - modern 敢
  - **interpretation:** The character 敢(gǎn, 'dare') evolved from an original depiction of a hand with a tool hunting a boar, signifying bravery or audacity. Over time, a capturing tool component was dropped, and minor strokes or components were added, resulting in the modern form.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )敢( )于(於)挑( )战(戰)权(權)威( )。
    - Tā gǎnyú tiǎozhàn quánwēi.
    - He dares to challenge authority.
  - 我( )不( )敢( )一( )个(個)人( )走( )那( )条(條)路( )。
    - Wǒ bù gǎn yī gèrén zǒu nà tiáo lù.
    - I don't dare to walk that road alone.
  - 如( )果( )有( )人( )敢( )欺( )负(負)你( )，就( )告( )诉(訴)我( )。
    - Rúguǒ yǒurén gǎn qīfù nǐ，jiù gàosù wǒ。
    - If anyone dares to bully you, just tell me.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 敢](@media/glyph6562.png)

### 敢 → 豕
- **definition:** boar
- **pinyin:** shǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a pig
  - **interpretation:** The character 豕(shǐ, "pig") directly depicts the side profile of a pig, with elements suggesting the animal's physical characteristics. This form visually represents the animal itself, making it easy to associate the character with the meaning of 'pig' or 'boar'.
- **examples:**
  - 古人用豕作( )为(為)祭( )品( )。
    - Gǔrén yòng shǐ zuòwéi jìpǐn.
    - The ancients used pigs as offerings.
  - 在( )山( )中( )，我( )们(們)发(發)现(現)了( )豕( )的( )踪(蹤)迹(跡)。
    - Zài shānzhōng, wǒmen fāxiànle shǐ de zōngjì.
    - In the mountains, we found traces of boars.
  - 他( )们(們)家( )养(養)了( )一( )些( )豕( )，用( )于(於)农(農)耕( )。
    - Tāmen jiā yǎngle yīxiē shǐ, yòng yú nónggēng.
    - Their family raised some pigs for farming.
- **historical forms:**

## 继(繼)续(續)
---
## continue; go on
### jìxù
---
- **traditional:** 繼續
- **definition:** continue; go on
- **pinyin:** jìxù
- **components:**
  - 继(繼)
    - jì
    - to continue; succeed; follow
  - 续(續)
    - xù
    - to continue; renew; connect; supply
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 繼 (jì, "to continue") connects the idea of proceeding after something has ended, like resuming a thread. 續 (xù, "to continue; renew") emphasizes the process of carrying something onwards, extending a sequence or action.
  - **interpretation:** 繼 (jì, "to continue") involves carrying on with something begun by another, akin to inheriting a task or position and moving forward. 續 (xù, "to continue; renew") builds on the concept of extending an action or maintaining continuity over time, suggesting seamless progression. Together, 繼續 (jìxù) creates a robust sense of unbroken continuation and maintaining momentum, ideal for depicting ongoing actions or processes.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )们(們)继(繼)续(續)工( )作( )。
    - Wǒmen jìxù gōngzuò.
    - We continue working.
  - 尽(儘)管( )下( )雨( )，他( )们(們)继(繼)续(續)比( )赛(賽)。
    - Jǐnguǎn xiàyǔ, tāmen jìxù bǐsài.
    - Despite the rain, they continue the game.
  - 他( )继(繼)续(續)学(學)习(習)中( )文( )。
    - Tā jìxù xuéxí Zhōngwén.
    - He continues to study Chinese.
### 继(繼)续(續) → 继(繼)
- **traditional:** 繼
- **definition:** to continue; succeed; follow
- **pinyin:** jì
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - silk; thread
  - 㡭
    - jì
    - coat, overcoat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 糸 (mì, "silk; thread") + 㡭 (jì) =
    - thread coming one after another ->
    - continue; follow; succeed
  - **interpretation:** In 繼, the component 糸 (mì, "silk; thread") suggests continuity, resembling threads being woven continuously. The phonetic element 㡭 (jì) provides the sound, aligning with the idea of succeeding or following. The original form possibly depicted multiple threads, reinforcing the notion of continuation.
  - **simplification:** The character 繼 was simplified to 继 by replacing the 糸 (mì, "silk; thread") with the simpler 纟, while retaining the phonetic value provided by 㡭.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )继(繼)承( )了( )父( )亲(親)的( )事( )业(業)。
    - Tā jìchéng le fùqīn de shìyè.
    - He succeeded his father's business.
  - 会(會)议(議)将(將)在( )午( )餐( )后(後)继(繼)续(續)。
    - Huìyì jiāng zài wǔcān hòu jìxù.
    - The meeting will continue after lunch.
  - 他( )们(們)制( )定( )了( )一( )个(個)继(繼)往( )开(開)来(來)的( )计(計)划(劃)。
    - Tāmen zhìdìng le yī gè jìwǎngkāilái de jìhuà.
    - They devised a plan to continue and innovate.
### 继(繼)续(續) → 继(繼) → 糸
- **definition:** silk; thread
- **pinyin:** mì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )手( )工( )制(製)作( )了( )一( )条(條)漂( )亮( )的( )丝(絲)巾( )。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)图(圖)必( )须(須)用( )细(細)糸( )画(畫)出( )来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我( )们(們)参(參)观(觀)了( )古( )代( )的( )织(織)布( )技( )术(術)，对(對)丝(絲)绸(綢)制(製)作( )产(產)生( )了( )兴(興)趣( )。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 糸](@media/glyph7cf8.png)
### 继(繼)续(續) → 继(繼) → 㡭
- **definition:** coat, overcoat
- **pinyin:** jì
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - silk; thread
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 糸 (mì, "silk; thread") + phonetic 㡭 (jì) ->
    - coat, overcoat; originally related to 繼 (jì, "to continue")
  - **interpretation:** The character 㡭 originally relates to 繼 (jì, "to continue"), where a thread weaves continuity. Here, it is used primarily for phonetic purposes, contributing its sound to the reading of 繼 but loses its original context when referencing a coat or overcoat.
### 继(繼)续(續) → 续(續)
- **traditional:** 續
- **definition:** to continue; renew; connect; supply
- **pinyin:** xù
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - sī
    - silk; thread
  - 𧶠
    - lù
    - to sell; trade
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 糸 (sī, "silk; thread") + 𧶠 (lù, "to sell; trade") =
    - thread-related concept with phonetic 𧶠 ->
    - continued threadwork
  - **interpretation:** The character combines the semantic element of 糸 (sī, "silk; thread") with the phonetic component 𧶠 (lù, "to sell; trade"), suggesting the idea of maintaining or extending a thread, symbolically extending or continuing something.
  - **simplification:** 續→续(續): 糸 (sī, "silk; thread") was simplified to 纟 as a stroke reduction, and 𧶠 was replaced by 卖 with fewer strokes while keeping phonetic resemblance.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )们(們)站( )在( )这(這)里(裡)聊( )天( )，然( )后(後)继(繼)续(續)前( )进(進)。
    - Wǒmen zhàn zài zhèlǐ liáotiān, ránhòu jìxù qiánjìn.
    - We stand here chatting, then continue moving forward.
  - 他( )决(決)定( )继(繼)续(續)他( )的( )研( )究( )。
    - Tā juédìng jìxù tā de yánjiū.
    - He decided to continue his research.
  - 即( )使( )遇( )到( )困( )难(難)，我( )们(們)也( )要( )继(繼)续(續)努( )力( )。
    - Jíshǐ yù dào kùnnán, wǒmen yě yào jìxù nǔlì.
    - Even when facing difficulties, we must continue to work hard.
### 继(繼)续(續) → 续(續) → 糸
- **definition:** silk; thread
- **pinyin:** sī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )手( )工( )制(製)作( )了( )一( )条(條)漂( )亮( )的( )丝(絲)巾( )。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)图(圖)必( )须(須)用( )细(細)糸( )画(畫)出( )来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我( )们(們)参(參)观(觀)了( )古( )代( )的( )织(織)布( )技( )术(術)，对(對)丝(絲)绸(綢)制(製)作( )产(產)生( )了( )兴(興)趣( )。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.
- **historical forms:**

### 继(繼)续(續) → 续(續) → 𧶠
- **definition:** to sell; trade
- **pinyin:** lù
- **components:**
  - 𡍬
    - mù
    - unknown phonetic
  - 貝
    - bèi
    - cowry
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𡍬 (phonetic) + 貝 (semantic, 'cowry') ->
    - means 'to sell; trade' ->
    - reduced to 士 and 四 in the current form
  - **interpretation:** The character combines the phonetic 𡍬, which later evolved into 士 (shì, 'scholar') and 四 (sì, 'four'), with the semantic 貝 (bèi, 'cowry'), symbolizing the concept of selling or trading goods, represented by the cowry shell.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 𧶠](@media/glyph27da0.png)
### 继(繼)续(續) → 续(續) → 𧶠 → 𡍬
- **definition:** unknown phonetic
- **pinyin:** mù
- **components:**
  - 圥
    - lù
    - "sound"
  - 囧
    - jiǒng
    - eye
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 圥("sound") + semantic 囧("eye") ->
    - a long time
  - **interpretation:** The character 𡍬 uses 圥 for its phonetic component to convey the sound and incorporates 囧, which depicts an 'eye', to suggest a visual or observational aspect that figuratively relates to the passage of 'a long time'. The idea is likely that something observed over a great period, as an eye might witness, conveys the meaning of duration.
### 继(繼)续(續) → 续(續) → 𧶠 → 𡍬 → 圥
- **definition:** "sound"
- **pinyin:** lù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant
  - **description:** 圥 is a variant form of 𡴆
  - **interpretation:** 圥 does not have its own distinct meaning; it serves as a variant form of 𡴆, likely used interchangeably in ancient texts.
### 继(繼)续(續) → 续(續) → 𧶠 → 𡍬 → 囧
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** jiǒng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a window with an open lattice pattern
  - **interpretation:** The character 囧(jǒng, "window") originally represents a window with an open lattice design, illustrating its functional purpose as a framework for ventilation and light.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)扇( )囧( )很( )大( )。
    - Zhè shàn jiǒng hěn dà.
    - This window is very large.
  - 早( )晨( )透( )过(過)囧( )射( )进(進)温(溫)暖( )的( )光( )，一( )切( )焕(煥)然( )一( )新( )。
    - Zǎochén tòuguò jiǒng shè jìn wēnnuǎn de guāng, yīqiè huànrán yīxīn.
    - In the morning, warm light poured in through the window, and everything looked brand new.
  - 老( )屋( )的( )囧( )保( )存( )着(著)历(歷)史( )的( )痕( )迹(跡)，诉(訴)说(說)着(著)往( )昔( )的( )故( )事( )。
    - Lǎowū de jiǒng bǎocún zhe lìshǐ de hénjì, sùshuō zhe wǎngxī de gùshì.
    - The old house's window preserves traces of history and tells stories of the past.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 囧](@media/glyph56e7.png)
### 继(繼)续(續) → 续(續) → 𧶠 → 貝
- **definition:** cowry
- **pinyin:** bèi
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a cowrie shell ->
    - used as currency in ancient China ->
    - stylized as 貝
  - **interpretation:** The character 貝(bèi, 'shell/money') visually represents a cowrie shell, which was used as a form of currency in ancient China. This explains why it is associated with money or valuables.
  - **simplification:** 贝 is a cursive script simplification of 貝, transforming the character into a more streamlined form while retaining its essence.
- **examples:**
  - 他把贝(貝)当作护(護)身( )符( )，放在口( )袋( )里(裡)。
    - Tā bǎ bèi dāng zuò hùshēn fú, fàng zài kǒudài lǐ.
    - He uses shells as a talisman, placing them in his pocket.
  - 古( )代( )人( )用( )贝(貝)作( )为(為)货(貨)币(幣)。
    - Gǔdài rén yòng bèi zuòwéi huòbì.
    - In ancient times, people used shells as currency.
