## 明信片
---
## postcard; lettercard
### míngxìnpiàn
---
- **definition:** postcard; lettercard
- **pinyin:** míngxìnpiàn
- **components:**
  - 明
    - míng
    - bright; clear
  - 信
    - xìn
    - letter; trust
  - 片
    - piàn
    - slice; piece
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 明 (míng, "bright"; "clear"), 信 (xìn, "letter"; "trust"), 片 (piàn, "slice"; "piece")
  - **interpretation:** A 明 (míng, "clear") 信 (xìn, "letter") that is a 片 (piàn, "piece") is a 'postcard', which is a clear message sent on a single piece of card.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )收( )到( )一( )张(張)明( )信( )片( )。
    - Wǒ shōudào yī zhāng míngxìnpiàn.
    - I received a postcard.
  - 旅行中我寄了明信片，向( )朋( )友( )问(問)候( )。
    - Lǚxíng zhōng wǒ jìle míngxìnpiàn, xiàng péngyǒu wènhòu.
    - During my trip, I mailed a postcard to greet my friend.
  - 旅( )行( )结(結)束( )时(時)我( )在( )包( )里(裡)发(發)现(現)了( )明( )信( )片( )，满(滿)载(載)回( )忆(憶)。
    - Lǚxíng jiéshù shí wǒ zài bāo lǐ fāxiànle míngxìnpiàn, mǎnzài huíyì.
    - At the end of the trip, I found a postcard in my bag, filled with memories.
### 明信片 → 明
- **definition:** bright; clear
- **pinyin:** míng
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, "sun") + 月 (yuè, "moon") =
    - sun is rising and moon not yet set ->
    - dawn ->
    - bright; other forms: 朙囧 + 月 =
    - moonlight, 眀目 + 月 =
    - bright eyes, 𤰾田 + 月 =
    - probable corruption
  - **interpretation:** The character combines the sun and moon, which both emit light, symbolizing brightness and clarity. Alternative forms reflect similar ideas related to light.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )意( )图(圖)明( )，所有人都能看出。
    - Tā de yìtú míng, suǒyǒu rén dōu néng kàn chū.
    - His intention is clear; everyone can tell.
  - 答案很明，无(無)需( )解( )释(釋)。
    - Dá'àn hěn míng, wúxū jiěshì.
    - The answer is obvious; no explanation is needed.
  - 会(會)议(議)内(內)容( )明( )，大( )家( )积(積)极(極)讨(討)论(論)。
    - Huìyì nèiróng míng, dàjiā jījí tǎolùn.
    - The content of the meeting is clear, and everyone engaged in active discussion.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 明](@media/glyph660e.png)
### 明信片 → 明 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨( )曦( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日( )出( )东(東)方( )。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖( )的( )日( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中( )午( )时(時)分( )，日( )高( )挂(掛)天( )。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 明信片 → 明 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜( )空( )挂(掛)着(著)明( )月( )。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人( )们(們)赏(賞)月( )，寄( )托(託)相( )思( )。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.

### 明信片 → 信
- **definition:** letter; trust
- **pinyin:** xìn
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 言
    - yán
    - words
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic: 人 (rén, "person") + Semantic: 言 (yán, "words") =
    - person speaking words ->
    - trust, letter, believe
  - **interpretation:** 信(xìn, "trust; letter; believe") combines 人 (rén, "person") as the phonetic element with 言 (yán, "words") to signify the concept of words spoken by a person, which relates to trust and belief. The presence of 言 emphasizes the communicative aspect, hence extending the meaning to include letters.
- **examples:**
  - 他信我，因( )为(為)我( )总(總)是( )守( )时(時)。
    - Tā xìn wǒ, yīnwèi wǒ zǒngshì shǒushí.
    - He trusts me because I am always punctual.
  - 我( )写(寫)信( )给(給)朋( )友( )。
    - Wǒ xiě xìn gěi péngyǒu.
    - I write a letter to a friend.
  - 请(請)信( )自( )己( )的( )选(選)择(擇)。
    - Qǐng xìn zìjǐ de xuǎnzé.
    - Please trust your own choices.
### 明信片 → 信 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )个(個)好( )人( )。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )有( )责(責)任( )，为(為)社( )会(會)作( )出( )贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心( )灵(靈)获(獲)得( )了( )成( )长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 人](@media/glyph4eba.png)
### 明信片 → 信 → 言
- **definition:** words
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 舌
    - shé
    - tongue
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 舌 (mouth with a forked tongue) with added stroke at top to suggest tongue movement ->
    - speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 言(yán, "speech") depicts the addition of a horizontal stroke to the ancient form of 舌(shé, "tongue") to indicate the motion of the tongue as it moves to articulate speech. This directly connects the organ involved in speaking to the concept of speech itself.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )言( )语(語)充( )满(滿)智( )慧( )。
    - Tā de yányǔ chōngmǎn zhìhuì.
    - His speech is full of wisdom.
  - 我( )们(們)应(應)该(該)以( )行( )动(動)证(證)明( )我( )们(們)的( )言( )词(詞)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi yǐ xíngdòng zhèngmíng wǒmen de yáncí.
    - We should prove our words with actions.
  - 他( )说(說)话(話)的( )方( )式( )显(顯)示( )了( )他( )的( )修( )养(養)。
    - Tā shuōhuà de fāngshì xiǎnshìle tā de xiūyǎng.
    - The way he speaks shows his refinement.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 言](@media/glyph8a00.png)
### 明信片 → 信 → 言 → 舌
- **definition:** tongue
- **pinyin:** shé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a forked tongue emerging upwards from a mouth
  - **interpretation:** The character 舌(shé, 'tongue') visually represents a tongue extending out from a mouth, which aligns with its meaning. This direct depiction makes it easy to remember its association with speech and taste in its semantic family, also relating to words like 言(yán, 'word').
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )舌( )非( )常( )灵(靈)敏( )。
    - Tā de shé fēicháng língmǐn.
    - His tongue is very sensitive.
  - 品( )尝(嚐)美( )食( )时(時)，他( )的( )舌( )细(細)品( )滋( )味( )。
    - Pǐncháng měishí shí, tā de shé xì pǐn zīwèi.
    - While tasting delicious food, his tongue savors every flavor.
  - 他( )长(長)舌( )无(無)忌( )，经(經)常( )泄( )露( )秘( )密( )。
    - Tā chángshé wújì, jīngcháng xièlòu mìmì.
    - He is talkative and often spills secrets.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 舌](@media/glyph820c.png)
### 明信片 → 信 → 言 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 口](@media/glyph53e3.png)
### 明信片 → 片
- **definition:** slice; piece
- **pinyin:** piàn
- **components:**
  - 爿
    - pán
    - piece
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood; tree
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Mirror image of 爿 (pán, 'piece'), which is the pictogram of a bed.
  - **interpretation:** 片 (piàn, 'slice; piece') is depicted as a mirror image of 爿 (pán, 'piece'), representing the concept of a slice or piece, visually similar to half of 木 (mù, 'wood; tree') to imply splitting or slicing.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )买(買)了( )一( )片( )面(麵)包( )。
    - Wǒ mǎile yī piàn miànbāo.
    - I bought a slice of bread.
  - 他( )摘( )下( )一( )片( )枫(楓)叶(葉)，轻(輕)轻(輕)放( )在( )桌( )上( )。
    - Tā zhāi xià yī piàn fēngyè, qīngqīng fàng zài zhuō shàng.
    - He picked a maple leaf and gently placed it on the table.
  - 天( )空( )中( )飘(飄)着( )一( )片( )白( )云(雲)。
    - Tiānkōng zhōng piāozhe yī piàn báiyún.
    - A patch of white cloud drifts across the sky.

### 明信片 → 片 → 爿
- **definition:** piece
- **pinyin:** pán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a bed ->
    - original form of 牀 (chuáng, "bed") ->
    - contracted form in 臧 (zāng, "possess")
  - **interpretation:** The character 爿 (pán, "bed") visually represents a bed, emphasizing its usage in denoting places for resting or sleeping. It served as the original form for the character 牀 (chuáng, "bed"), reinforcing its meaning. Additionally, in the character 臧 (zāng, "possess"), it appears as a contracted form, reflecting its historical usage in composite forms.

### 明信片 → 片 → 木

  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把( )椅( )子( )的( )主( )要( )材( )料( )是( )木( )。

## 面前
---
## in front of
### miànqián
---
- **definition:** in front of
- **pinyin:** miànqián
- **components:**
  - 面
    - miàn
    - face; surface; side; aspect
  - 前
    - qián
    - front; ahead; before; future
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 面 (miàn, "face") refers to the front or surface; 前 (qián, "front") indicates a position that is before something.
  - **interpretation:** 面 (miàn, "face") signifies the side of something that is outward or forward-facing, i.e., the front aspect. 前 (qián, "front") intrinsically means ahead or in position before something. When combined, they intuitively form the notion of 'in front of' by positioning 'face' at 'the front', specifying the area directly before a reference point.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )站( )在( )镜(鏡)子( )面( )前( )。
    - Tā zhàn zài jìngzi miànqián.
    - He stands in front of the mirror.
  - 在( )观(觀)众(眾)面( )前( )表( )演( )，让(讓)我( )感( )到( )紧(緊)张(張)。
    - Zài guānzhòng miànqián biǎoyǎn, ràng wǒ gǎndào jǐnzhāng.
    - Performing in front of an audience makes me nervous.
  - 雨( )后(後)，彩( )虹( )出( )现(現)在( )我( )们(們)面( )前( )。
    - Yǔ hòu, cǎihóng chūxiàn zài wǒmen miànqián.
    - After the rain, a rainbow appeared in front of us.
### 面前 → 面
- **definition:** face; surface; side; aspect
- **pinyin:** miàn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a man's face, with an eye exaggerated, derived from 𦣻; the horizontal stroke was added later
  - **interpretation:** The character 面(miàn, "face") visually represents a person's face with an exaggerated eye, highlighting the frontal aspect of the head. The design was later complemented by a horizontal stroke to complete its pictorial depiction.
  - **simplification:** In the case of 麵, the component 麥 (mài, "wheat") was eliminated to simplify the character, resulting in 面 being used as the sole representation.
- **examples:**
  - 她的面容总(總)是( )带(帶)着(著)微( )笑( )。
    - Tā de miànróng zǒng shì dài zhe wéixiào.
    - Her face always wears a smile.
  - 这(這)个(個)湖( )的( )表( )面( )很( )平( )静(靜)。
    - Zhège hú de biǎomiàn hěn píngjìng.
    - The surface of this lake is very calm.
  - 他( )面( )对(對)困( )难(難)毫( )不( )退( )缩(縮)。
    - Tā miànduì kùnnán háo bù tuìsuō.
    - He faces difficulties without retreating.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 面](@media/glyph9762.png)
### 面前 → 前
- **definition:** front; ahead; before; future
- **pinyin:** qián
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 舟
    - zhōu
    - boat
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 剪
    - jiǎn
    - to cut
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止 (zhǐ, 'foot') + 舟 (zhōu, 'boat') =
    - foot on a boat moving forward ->
    - 止 simplified to 䒑 and 舟 to 月 with 刀 (dāo, 'knife') added
  - **interpretation:** Originally, 前 depicted a foot moving a boat forward, symbolizing advance or progress. Later, components were simplified and a knife was added, linking to its historical connection as the original form of 剪 (jiǎn, 'to cut').
- **examples:**
  - 我站在房子前面。
    - Wǒ zhàn zài fángzi qiánmiàn.
    - I am standing in front of the house.
  - 前( )几(幾)天( )我( )去( )北( )京( )旅( )游(遊)。
    - Qián jǐ tiān wǒ qù Běijīng lǚyóu.
    - A few days ago, I went to Beijing for a trip.
  - 他比我到得更早，已( )经(經)在( )咖( )啡( )店( )前( )等( )我( )。
    - Tā bǐ wǒ dào de gèng zǎo, yǐjīng zài kāfēidiàn qián děng wǒ.
    - He arrived earlier than me and was already waiting for me in front of the café.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 前](@media/glyph524d.png)
### 面前 → 前 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)的( )止( )需( )要( )静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他( )走( )路( )时(時)小( )心( )谨(謹)慎( )，因( )为(爲)止( )若( )受( )伤(傷)便( )难(難)前( )行( )。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 止](@media/glyph6b62.png)
### 面前 → 前 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )脚(腳)趾( )受( )伤(傷)了( )。
    - Tā de jiǎozhǐ shòushāng le.
    - His toe is injured.
  - 她( )用( )脚(腳)趾( )轻(輕)轻(輕)地( )踢( )了( )一( )下( )球( )。
    - Tā yòng jiǎozhǐ qīngqīng de tī le yīxià qiú.
    - She gently kicked the ball with her toe.
  - 在( )沙( )滩(灘)上( )散( )步( )时(時)，我( )感( )受( )到( )沙( )子( )在( )我( )的( )脚(腳)趾( )间(間)流( )动(動)。
    - Zài shātān shàng sànbù shí, wǒ gǎnshòu dào shāzi zài wǒ de jiǎozhǐ jiān liúdòng.
    - While walking on the beach, I felt the sand flowing between my toes.
### 面前 → 前 → 止 → 趾 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)后(後)，他( )的( )足( )不( )能( )动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小( )明( )打( )球( )时(時)，不( )小( )心( )扭( )伤(傷)了( )足( )。
    - xiǎo míng dǎ qiú shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ shāng le zú。
    - When Xiaoming was playing ball, he accidentally twisted his foot.
  - 我( )每( )天( )锻(鍛)炼(鍊)足( )部( )。
    - wǒ měitiān duànliàn zúbù。
    - I exercise my foot muscles every day.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 足](@media/glyph8db3.png)
### 面前 → 前 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 面前 → 前 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )手( )写(寫)字( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我( )的( )手( )走( )路( )。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他( )的( )手( )很( )温(溫)暖( )，带(帶)给(給)我( )力( )量( )。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
- **historical forms:**

### 面前 → 前 → 舟

  - **type:** pictogram

  - **interpretation:** The character 舟 (zhōu, "boat") visually represents the outline of a boat, reflecting its function and form.
- **examples:**

    - Qīngchén shífèn zhōu zài xíngrén, chuānguò gǔzhèn héliú.
    - In the early morning, the boat carries passengers as it passes through the ancient town's river.

### 面前 → 前 → 刀
- **definition:** knife
- **pinyin:** dāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )锋(鋒)利( )的( )刀( )，切( )开(開)蔬( )菜( )。
    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.
    - He uses a sharp knife to cut vegetables.
  - 这(這)把( )刀( )非( )常( )锋(鋒)利( )。
    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.
  - 厨(廚)师(師)小( )心( )地( )持( )刀( )，为(為)客( )人( )切( )肉( )。
    - chúshī xiǎoxīn de chí dāo, wèi kèrén qiē ròu.
    - The chef holds the knife carefully and slices meat for the guest.

### 面前 → 前 → 剪
- **definition:** to cut
- **pinyin:** jiǎn
- **components:**
  - 前
    - qián
    - before
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 歬
    - qián
    - advance, move forward
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𣦃 (original) ->
    - stylized as 前 (phonetic 歬 + semantic 刀) ->
    - 前 replaced 歬; extra 刀 added ->
    - final form 剪
  - **interpretation:** Initially represented by 𣦃 and later evolved by stylization into 前 with a phonetic component 歬 and a semantic component 刀 (a knife). To retain the semantic connection with cutting, an additional 刀 component was added after the phonetic part was replaced by 前.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )用( )剪( )刀( )剪( )纸(紙)。
    - Tā yòng jiǎndāo jiǎn zhǐ.
    - She uses scissors to cut paper.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)帮(幫)我( )剪( )头(頭)发(髮)。
    - Māma bāng wǒ jiǎn tóufà.
    - Mom helps me cut my hair.
  - 他( )喜( )欢(歡)剪( )小( )说(說)中( )的( )插( )图(圖)。
    - Tā xǐhuān jiǎn xiǎoshuō zhōng de chātú.
    - He likes to cut illustrations from novels.
### 面前 → 前 → 剪 → 歬
- **definition:** advance, move forward
- **pinyin:** qián
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 舟
    - zhōu
    - boat
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 止 (zhǐ, "foot") + phonetic 舟 (zhōu) ->
    - moving forward (by foot on a boat)
  - **interpretation:** Originally, 歬 (qián) ("advance, move forward") combined a foot 止 (zhǐ, "foot") and a boat 舟 (zhōu, "boat") to symbolize movement, as one would advance by stepping onto a boat. This imagery conveys the concept of advancing or moving forward in a dynamic, physical manner.

## in front of

## 金字塔
---
## pyramid
### jīnzìtǎ
---
- **definition:** pyramid
- **pinyin:** jīnzìtǎ
- **components:**
  - 金
    - jīn
    - gold; metal; money
  - 字
    - zì
    - character; word; letter
  - 塔
    - tǎ
    - tower; pagoda; steeple
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 金 (jīn, "gold") + 字 (zì, "character; word; writing") + 塔 (tǎ, "tower; pagoda") =
    - a structure shaped like a character made of gold ->
    - pyramid
  - **interpretation:** 金 (jīn, "gold") suggests preciousness and value, hinting at the grandeur and historical reverence for pyramids. 字 (zì, "character") conveys the idea of form or shape, analogous to how a pyramid has a distinctive, recognizable form. 塔 (tǎ, "tower") represents a tall, structured form, reflecting the towering shape of a pyramid. Combined, the word captures a sense of an esteemed, shaped structure, which accords with the pyramids' dimensions and esteemed historical and cultural role.
- **examples:**
  - 在( )埃( )及( )有( )许(許)多( )著( )名( )的( )金( )字( )塔( )。
    - Zài Āijí yǒu xǔduō zhùmíng de jīnzìtǎ.
    - There are many famous pyramids in Egypt.
  - 科( )学(學)家( )正( )在( )研( )究( )金( )字( )塔( )的( )建( )造( )方( )法( )。
    - Kēxuéjiā zhèngzài yánjiū jīnzìtǎ de jiànzào fāngfǎ.
    - Scientists are studying the construction methods of pyramids.
  - 金( )字( )塔( )是( )古( )代( )文( )明( )的( )伟(偉)大( )象( )征(徵)。
    - Jīnzìtǎ shì gǔdài wénmíng de wěidà xiàngzhēng.
    - The pyramid is a great symbol of ancient civilizations.
### 金字塔 → 金
- **definition:** gold; metal; money
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 士
    - shì
    - upside-down ritual axe
  - 呂
    - lǚ
    - two blocks of metal
  - 亼
    - jí
    - open mouth upside down
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 士 (upside-down ritual axe) + 呂 (two blocks of metal) + phonetic 亼 (open mouth upside down) ->
    - original pronunciation; no earth pictogram in ancient forms ->
    - metal, later gold
  - **interpretation:** Initially representing copper, due to its use in the Copper Age, the character 金 (jīn, "metal") evolved to refer broadly to metal as technological progress made various metals crucial in society. The extension to gold reflects its value and prominence. The phonetic 亼 indicates the character's pronunciation, with semantic elements showing early associations with precious materials.
- **examples:**
  - 金( )是( )一( )种(種)重( )要( )的( )工( )业(業)原( )料( )。
    - Jīn shì yī zhǒng zhòngyào de gōngyè yuánliào.
    - Metal is an important industrial material.
  - 她( )的( )项(項)链(鍊)是( )纯(純)金( )的( )。
    - Tā de xiàngliàn shì chún jīn de.
    - Her necklace is made of pure gold.
  - 每( )个(個)国(國)家( )都( )有( )自( )己( )的( )金( )矿(礦)。
    - Měi gè guójiā dōu yǒu zìjǐ de jīnkuàng.
    - Every country has its own gold mines.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 金](@media/glyph91d1.png)
### 金字塔 → 金 → 士
- **definition:** upside-down ritual axe
- **pinyin:** shì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a ritual axe, possibly made of jade ->
    - symbolized soldier ->
    - intellectual or officer over time
  - **interpretation:** The character 士(shì, 'scholar') originally depicted a ritual axe used in ceremonies, implying a person of a certain rank or status who could wield such symbols. This connection to ceremonial authority evolved to mean 'soldier' and later 'intellectual' or 'officer', roles associated with leadership and knowledge in societal hierarchies.
- **examples:**
  - 历(歷)史( )上( )，士( )被( )视(視)为(為)一( )种(種)权(權)力( )的( )象( )征(徵)。
    - Lìshǐ shàng, shì bèi shì wéi yī zhǒng quánlì de xiàngzhēng.
    - Historically, the 'shi' was seen as a symbol of power.
  - 在( )古( )代( )，只( )有( )贵(貴)族( )才( )拥(擁)有( )士( )。
    - Zài gǔdài, zhǐyǒu guìzú cái yǒngyǒu shì.
    - In ancient times, only nobles possessed the 'shi'.
  - 士( )的( )制(製)作( )材( )料( )可( )能( )是( )珍( )贵(貴)的( )金( )属(屬)。
    - Shì de zhìzuò cáiliào kěnéng shì zhēnguì de jīnshǔ.
    - The materials used to make the 'shi' might have been precious metals.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 士](@media/glyph58eb.png)
### 金字塔 → 金 → 呂
- **definition:** two blocks of metal
- **pinyin:** lǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two disconnected blocks of metal, later connected in seal script ->
    - Original form of 鋁 (lǚ, 'ingot') ->
    - Borrowed phonetically for 'spine' and 'music notes'
  - **interpretation:** The character 呂(lǚ) ('two blocks of metal') visually represents two separate blocks aligned vertically. In its earliest forms, these blocks were disconnected, symbolizing distinct metal segments, which aligns with its early use for 'ingot'. Over time, as seen in seal script, a connecting line was added to form the modern appearance. This visual interpretation supports its original meaning related to metal. It was later phonetically borrowed to convey concepts like 'spine' and 'music notes', where no direct semantic link exists with metal, but the sound similarity allowed its reuse in these contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )两(兩)个(個)大( )的( )金( )属(屬)块(塊)铸(鑄)造( )了( )一( )个(個)雕( )像( )。
    - Tā yòng liǎng gè dà de jīnshǔ kuài zhùzào le yī gè diāoxiàng.
    - He cast a statue using two large blocks of metal.
  - 现(現)代( )工( )业(業)中( )，金( )属(屬)块(塊)常( )用( )于(於)制(製)造( )重( )型( )设(設)备(備)。
    - Xiàndài gōngyè zhōng, jīnshǔ kuài cháng yòng yú zhìzào zhòngxíng shèbèi.
    - In modern industry, metal blocks are often used for manufacturing heavy equipment.
  - 这(這)个(個)设(設)计(計)师(師)用( )金( )属(屬)块(塊)建( )造( )了( )一( )个(個)现(現)代( )化( )建( )筑(築)。
    - Zhège shèjì shī yòng jīnshǔ kuài jiànzào le yī gè xiàndàihuà jiànzhù.
    - The designer built a modern structure using metal blocks.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 呂](@media/glyph5442.png)
### 金字塔 → 金 → 亼
- **definition:** open mouth upside down
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)

    - collect; assemble

  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.

### 金字塔 → 字

    - mián

    - child under a roof ->
    - representation of how children would learn to write characters inside a house ->
    - character
  - **interpretation:** The character 字(zì, "character") combines 子(zǐ, "child") and 宀(mián, "roof") to depict a child learning to write under the protection of a roof. This makes intuitive sense as learning and education traditionally took place at home.
- **examples:**

  - **description:**
    - Depicts a house with four walls ->
    - roof
  - **interpretation:** 宀(mián, "roof") is a pictogram representing a house with four walls. It emphasizes an enclosed space, distinguishing it from similar structures like 广(guǎng, "broad") which depicts a building with three walls. This makes 宀 a logical choice for representing a roof in various characters.
- **examples:**

    - Wūdǐng zhē fēng dǎng yǔ, jiāyuán sànfā wēnxīn.
    - The roof shields from wind and rain, and the home radiates warmth.

### 金字塔 → 塔 → 荅 → 合 → 亼 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )一( )个(個)苹(蘋)果( )。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他( )只( )看( )到( )一( )只(隻)鸟(鳥)，飞(飛)进(進)了( )花( )园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一( )条(條)直( )路( )通( )向( )远(遠)方( )。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.

### 金字塔 → 塔 → 荅 → 合 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )的( )天( )气(氣)不( )错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.

    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.

    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 金字塔 → 塔 → 荅 → 合 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.

    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.

    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.

## 记(記)得( )
---
## remember
### jìde
---
- **traditional:** 記得
- **definition:** remember
- **pinyin:** jìde
- **components:**
  - 记(記)
    - jì
    - record; remember
  - 得
    - dé
    - obtain; get
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 記 (jì, "record; remember") and 得 (dé, "obtain; get") together convey the idea of "successfully recording in one's mind," thus meaning "to remember."
  - **interpretation:** This combination makes sense because 記 (jì, "record; remember") implies the act of noting information mentally, while 得 (dé, "obtain; get") indicates the successful acquisition of this memory.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)记(記)得( )锁(鎖)门(門)。
    - Qǐng jìde suǒ mén.
    - Please remember to lock the door.
  - 你( )还(還)记(記)得( )那( )次( )旅( )行( )吗(嗎)？
    - Nǐ hái jìde nà cì lǚxíng ma?
    - Do you still remember that trip?
  - 他( )让(讓)我( )记(記)得( )带(帶)伞(傘)。
    - Tā ràng wǒ jìde dài sǎn.
    - He asked me to remember to bring an umbrella.
### 记(記)得( ) → 记(記)
- **traditional:** 記
- **definition:** record; remember
- **pinyin:** jì
- **components:**
  - 言
    - yán
    - speech
  - 己
    - jǐ
    - self
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 言 (yán, "speech; words") + 己 (jǐ, "self") =
    - speech related to oneself ->
    - final form 記
  - **interpretation:** The character 記 (jì, "record") combines speech 言, indicating communication or words, with the phonetic 己, referring to oneself. This combination suggests the idea of recording or remembering words related to oneself or one's experiences.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 記 was simplified to 记 by replacing 言(言, "speech") with the simpler 讠, reducing stroke count while maintaining the semantic component.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )每( )天( )写(寫)日( )记(記)。
    - Wǒ měitiān xiě rìjì.
    - I write a diary every day.
  - 请(請)记(記)住( )这(這)条(條)重( )要( )的( )规(規)则(則)。
    - Qǐng jì zhù zhè tiáo zhòngyào de guīzé.
    - Please remember this important rule.
  - 他( )把( )电(電)话(話)号(號)码(碼)记(記)在( )本( )子( )上( )。
    - Tā bǎ diànhuà hàomǎ jì zài běnzi shàng.
    - He recorded the phone number in the notebook.
### 记(記)得( ) → 记(記) → 言
- **definition:** speech
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 舌
    - shé
    - tongue
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 舌 (mouth with a forked tongue) with added stroke at top to suggest tongue movement ->
    - speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 言(yán, "speech") depicts the addition of a horizontal stroke to the ancient form of 舌(shé, "tongue") to indicate the motion of the tongue as it moves to articulate speech. This directly connects the organ involved in speaking to the concept of speech itself.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )言( )语(語)充( )满(滿)智( )慧( )。
    - Tā de yányǔ chōngmǎn zhìhuì.
    - His speech is full of wisdom.
  - 我( )们(們)应(應)该(該)以( )行( )动(動)证(證)明( )我( )们(們)的( )言( )词(詞)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi yǐ xíngdòng zhèngmíng wǒmen de yáncí.
    - We should prove our words with actions.
  - 他( )说(說)话(話)的( )方( )式( )显(顯)示( )了( )他( )的( )修( )养(養)。
    - Tā shuōhuà de fāngshì xiǎnshìle tā de xiūyǎng.
    - The way he speaks shows his refinement.

### 记(記)得( ) → 记(記) → 己 → 紀
- **definition:** record
- **pinyin:** jì
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - silk; thread
  - 己
    - jǐ
    - self

  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') + phonetic 己 (jǐ) ->
    - record
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') indicating threads or lines, with 己 (jǐ) as the phonetic component. In this context, 'thread' aligns with 'record' in the sense of a sequence or line of events documented over time.
  - **simplification:** The traditional form 紀 with 糸 (mì, 'silk; thread') replaced by the simpler 纟 in the simplified form 纪.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)本( )书(書)详(詳)细(細)记(記)录(錄)了( )历(歷)史( )事( )件( )。

    - Gōngsī zài niándǐ huì fābù niándù bàogào lái jìlù fāzhǎn qíngkuàng.
    - The company will release an annual report at the end of the year to record development status.

### 记(記)得( ) → 得
- **definition:** obtain; get
- **pinyin:** dé
- **components:**
  - 貝
    - bèi
    - cowry
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 彳
    - chì
    - step
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
  - 旦
    - dàn
    - dawn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 貝 (bèi, 'cowry') + 又 (yòu, 'hand') ->
    - obtaining valuables ->
    - 彳 (chì, 'step') added, 又 changed to 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), 貝 corrupted to 旦 (dàn, 'dawn') ->
    - final form
  - **interpretation:** The character originated as a depiction of a hand picking up a cowry, symbolizing 'obtaining' valuables. The 彳 (chì, 'step') was added to suggest movement on a road, enhancing the idea of acquisition. Over time, script evolutions saw substitute elements: the component 又 (yòu, 'hand') changed to 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), reflecting the Qin script's tendency, and 貝 (bèi, 'cowry') was simplified to 旦 (dàn, 'dawn'). These changes led to the character's modern form. This transition mirrors the evolved meanings in usage: 'to get', from obtaining something physically; 'must', representing the necessity of movement or action; and its role as a structural particle in grammar for completion or necessity in expressions.
  - **simplification:** In simplified form, 得 remains unchanged from its traditional representation.
- **examples:**
  - 他跑得很快。
    - Tā pǎo de hěn kuài.
    - He runs very fast.
  - 我得去工作。
    - Wǒ děi qù gōngzuò.
    - I have to go to work.
  - 她( )昨( )天( )赢(贏)得( )了( )比( )赛(賽)。
    - Tā zuótiān yíngdé le bǐsài.
    - She won the competition yesterday.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 得](@media/glyph5f97.png)
### 记(記)得( ) → 得 → 貝
- **definition:** cowry
- **pinyin:** bèi
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a cowrie shell ->
    - used as currency in ancient China ->
    - stylized as 貝
  - **interpretation:** The character 貝(bèi, 'shell/money') visually represents a cowrie shell, which was used as a form of currency in ancient China. This explains why it is associated with money or valuables.
  - **simplification:** 贝 is a cursive script simplification of 貝, transforming the character into a more streamlined form while retaining its essence.
- **examples:**
  - 他把贝(貝)当作护(護)身( )符( )，放在口( )袋( )里(裡)。
    - Tā bǎ bèi dāng zuò hùshēn fú, fàng zài kǒudài lǐ.
    - He uses shells as a talisman, placing them in his pocket.
  - 古( )代( )人( )用( )贝(貝)作( )为(為)货(貨)币(幣)。
    - Gǔdài rén yòng bèi zuòwéi huòbì.
    - In ancient times, people used shells as currency.
### 记(記)得( ) → 得 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又( )」这(這)个(個)字( )最( )早( )来(來)源( )于(於)手( )。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很( )多( )汉(漢)字( )含( )有( )又( )部( )首( )，表( )示( )与(與)手( )有( )关(關)的( )动(動)作( )。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古( )人( )用( )又( )描( )绘(繪)手( )的( )形( )态(態)，体(體)现(現)了( )古( )汉(漢)字( )的( )独(獨)特( )魅( )力( )。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.

### 记(記)得( ) → 得 → 彳

### 记(記)得( ) → 得 → 寸
- **definition:** inch
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)块(塊)布( )每( )一( )寸( )都( )是( )精( )心( )制(製)作( )。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用( )卷( )尺( )量( )一( )寸( )，每( )一( )寸( )数(數)据(據)都( )准(準)确(確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寸](@media/glyph5bf8.png)
### 记(記)得( ) → 得 → 旦
- **definition:** dawn
- **pinyin:** dàn
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 丁
    - dīng
    - nail
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, "sun") + 丁 (dīng, "nail") =
    - sun appearing over the horizon, 丁 indicates pronunciation
  - **interpretation:** Although the original interpretation is debated, the character combines 日 (rì, "sun") and 丁 (dīng, "nail") to depict the sun rising. This is a visual representation of dawn, where the sun emerges at the horizon line.
- **examples:**
  - 破( )晓(曉)的( )旦( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)山( )川( )。
    - Pòxiǎo de dàn guāng sǎ mǎn shānchuān.
    - The light of dawn scattered over the mountains and rivers.
  - 黎( )明( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，旦( )光( )映( )红(紅)天( )边(邊)。
    - Límíng láilín shí, dàn guāng yìng hóng tiānbiān.
    - When dawn arrives, the light of dawn paints the sky red.
  - 在( )寂( )静(靜)的( )山( )谷( )中( )，天( )边(邊)的( )旦( )光( )预(預)告( )着(著)新( )生( )。
    - Zài jìjìng de shāngǔ zhōng, tiānbiān de dàn guāng yùgào zhe xīnshēng.
    - In the quiet valley, the light of dawn heralds new life.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 旦](@media/glyph65e6.png)
### 记(記)得( ) → 得 → 旦 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨( )曦( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，日( )出( )东(東)方( )。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖( )的( )日( )光( )洒(灑)满(滿)大( )地( )。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中( )午( )时(時)分( )，日( )高( )挂(掛)天( )。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 日](@media/glyph65e5.png)
### 记(記)得( ) → 得 → 旦 → 丁
- **definition:** nail
- **pinyin:** dīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of a nail ->
    - 丁
  - **interpretation:** The character 丁 originally depicted the head of a nail, emphasizing simplicity and directness. While it has developed other interpretations over time, such as a head or city wall, these relate to similar shapes and functions. Today, 釘 (dīng, 'nail') reflects this meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 工( )人( )熟( )练(練)地( )把( )丁( )敲( )进(進)了( )墙(牆)壁( )。
    - Gōngrén shúliàn de bǎ dīng qiāng jìnle qiángbì.
    - The worker skillfully hammered the nail into the wall.
  - 他( )精( )心( )挑( )选(選)了( )铁(鐵)质(質)丁( )，确(確)保( )家(傢)具(俱)稳(穩)固( )。
    - Tā jīngxīn tiāoxuǎnle tiě zhì dīng, quèbǎo jiājù wěngù.
    - He carefully selected the iron nail to ensure the furniture was stable.
  - 请(請)把( )散( )落( )的( )丁( )收( )好( )。
    - Qǐng bǎ sànluò de dīng shōuhǎo.
    - Please gather the scattered nails.
- **historical forms:**

## 小( )时(時)候( )
---
## childhood
### xiǎoshíhou
---
- **traditional:** 小時候
- **definition:** childhood
- **pinyin:** xiǎoshíhou
- **components:**
  - 小
    - xiǎo
    - small; little; young; minor
  - 時候
    - shíhou
    - time; moment; period; while
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 小 (xiǎo, "small") + 時候 (shíhou, "time; moment") indicates a period of life marked by small size or youth. "Childhood" conveys the idea of the time when one is small in stature and age.
  - **interpretation:** 小 (xiǎo, "small") refers to being young, as children are smaller in size. 時候 (shíhou, "time; moment") points to a specific period. Together, 小時候 (xiǎoshíhou) intuitively refers to the 'time of being small,' signifying childhood when individuals are young and growing.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )小( )时(時)候( )常( )常( )去( )爷(爺)爷(爺)家( )玩( )。
    - Wǒ xiǎoshíhou chángcháng qù yéye jiā wán.
    - I often went to my grandpa's house to play during my childhood.
  - 小( )时(時)候( )的( )回( )忆(憶)总(總)是( )很( )美( )好( )。
    - Xiǎoshíhou de huíyì zǒng shì hěn měihǎo.
    - Memories of childhood are always very beautiful.
  - 他( )小( )时(時)候( )特( )别(別)喜( )欢(歡)看( )书(書)，现(現)在( )也( )不( )例( )外( )。
    - Tā xiǎoshíhou tèbié xǐhuan kànshū, xiànzài yě bù lìwài.
    - He especially liked reading during his childhood, and it's still the same now.
### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 小
- **definition:** small; little; young; minor
- **pinyin:** xiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts three small dots arranged symmetrically to represent something small
  - **interpretation:** The character 小(xiǎo, 'small') uses three small strokes to symbolize size or quantity, visually capturing the essence of 'smallness'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小( )猫(貓)很( )可( )爱(愛)。
    - Zhège xiǎo māo hěn kě'ài.
    - This small cat is very cute.
  - 这(這)座( )小( )桥(橋)横(橫)跨( )河( )流( )，连(連)接( )两(兩)岸( )。
    - Zhè zuò xiǎo qiáo héngkuà héliú, liánjiē liǎng àn.
    - This small bridge spans the river, connecting both banks.
  - 请(請)给(給)我( )一( )小( )杯( )水( )。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ yī xiǎo bēi shuǐ.
    - Please give me a small cup of water.

### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候
- **definition:** time; moment; period; while
- **pinyin:** shíhou
- **components:**
  - 時
    - shí
    - time; hour; period
  - 候
    - hòu
    - wait; moment; time; period
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 時 (shí, "time; hour; period") refers to a specific point in time or a duration. 候 (hòu, "wait; moment") indicates a time or a period during which something can occur.
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 時 (shí, "time; hour; period") and 候 (hòu, "wait; moment") suggests a span of time or a specific moment when something happens. It reflects how a moment is both a point and a period in time.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )走( )的( )时(時)候( )，天( )已( )经(經)黑( )了( )。
    - Wǒ zǒu de shíhòu, tiān yǐjīng hēi le.
    - By the time I left, it was already dark.
  - 上( )学(學)的( )时(時)候( )，他( )喜( )欢(歡)写(寫)作( )。
    - Shàngxué de shíhòu, tā xǐhuān xiězuò.
    - When he was in school, he liked writing.
  - 你( )什( )么(麼)时(時)候( )回( )来(來)？
    - Nǐ shénme shíhòu huílái?
    - When will you come back?
### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 時
- **definition:** time; hour; period
- **pinyin:** shí
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 寺
    - sì
    - temple
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, "sun") + 寺 (sì, "temple") as phonetic =
    - time marker influenced by the sun's movement ->
    - 寸 (cùn, "inch") added in associated compound
  - **interpretation:** The character 時(shí, "time") combines the semantic element 日 (rì, "sun") with the phonetic element 寺 (sì, "temple"). The concept of measuring time relates to the sun's movement; 寸 (cùn, "inch") later added emphasized the notion of time as a measurable entity.
  - **simplification:** The simplified character 时 is a cursive handwritten variant of 時, streamlined by omitting the 寸 component.
- **examples:**
  - 时(時)间(間)就( )是( )金( )钱(錢)。
    - Shíjiān jiùshì jīnqián.
    - Time is money.
  - 每( )当(當)我( )想( )你( )时(時)，心( )情( )就( )会(會)变(變)好( )。
    - Měidāng wǒ xiǎng nǐ shí, xīnqíng jiù huì biàn hǎo.
    - Whenever I think of you, my mood improves.
  - 雨( )季( )来(來)临(臨)时(時)，我( )们(們)需( )要( )准(準)备(備)好( )雨( )具( )。
    - Yǔjì láilín shí, wǒmen xūyào zhǔnbèi hǎo yǔjù.
    - When the rainy season arrives, we need to prepare our rain gear.
- **historical forms:**

### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 時 → 寺
- **definition:** temple
- **pinyin:** sì
- **components:**
  - 𡳿
    - zhī
    - to go; footprint
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - inch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 𡳿 ->
    - 之; 士 + semantic 又 (hand) ->
    - 寸 in Small Seal Script ->
    - 寺
  - **interpretation:** 寺(sì, 'temple') combines the semantic element 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), originally from 又 (yòu, 'hand'), to imply precision or holding, with the phonetic element that evolved into 士 (shì, 'scholar'). The phonetic component originally represented going or movement but later took on a more abstract form. This combination suggests a place of order and ritual, characteristic of temples.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )每( )天( )早( )晨( )去( )寺( )庙(廟)。
    - Tā měitiān zǎochén qù sìmiào.
    - He goes to the temple every morning.
  - 寺( )庙(廟)里(裡)的( )钟(鐘)声(聲)非( )常( )悠( )扬(揚)。
    - Sìmiào lǐ de zhōngshēng fēicháng yōuyáng.
    - The bell sounds in the temple are very melodious.
  - 我( )们(們)参(參)观(觀)了( )京( )都( )的( )古( )老( )寺( )庙(廟)，觉(覺)得( )很( )平( )静(靜)。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle Jīngdū de gǔlǎo sìmiào, juéde hěn píngjìng.
    - We visited an ancient temple in Kyoto and felt very peaceful.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 寺](@media/glyph5bfa.png)
### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 時 → 寺 → 𡳿
- **definition:** to go; footprint
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 一
    - yī
    - the beginning place
  - 之
    - zhī
    - to go
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止(“foot”) + 一(“the beginning place”) ->
    - originally 㞢 ->
    - similar to 出 ->
    - evolved as a variant of 之
  - **interpretation:** The character 𡳿 is a variant of 之 (zhī, "to go") and conveys the idea of movement or direction. The original form 㞢 combines 止 (zhǐ, "foot") representing a footprint with 一 (yī, "the beginning place"), symbolizing the commencement of movement or journey, leading to the meaning of 'to go'. Over time, components such as the footprint evolved into different forms, leading to variants such as 𡳿.
### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 時 → 寺 → 𡳿 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)的( )止( )需( )要( )静(靜)养(養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他( )走( )路( )时(時)小( )心( )谨(謹)慎( )，因( )为(爲)止( )若( )受( )伤(傷)便( )难(難)前( )行( )。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.

### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 時 → 寺 → 𡳿 → 一

- **pinyin:** yī

  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.

### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 時 → 寺 → 𡳿 → 之
- **definition:** to go
- **pinyin:** zhī
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 一
    - yī
    - one; the beginning place
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止 ('foot') + 一 ('beginning place') ->
    - originally 㞢 ('to go') ->
    - simplified to a point
  - **interpretation:** The original compound 㞢 depicted a foot 止 (zhǐ, 'foot') stepping on a line 一 (yī, 'one; the beginning place'), indicating the concept of 'to go'. The footprint evolving into a point symbolized direction or movement, ultimately abstracted into 之 (zhī, 'of; possessive particle'), representing directionality or connection, as in 'of'.
- **examples:**
  - 天( )空( )之( )蓝(藍)让(讓)人( )心( )旷(曠)神( )怡( )。
    - Tiānkōng zhī lán ràng rén xīnkuàngshényí.
    - The blue of the sky makes people feel relaxed and happy.
  - 树(樹)之( )影( )在( )湖( )面( )上( )摇(搖)曳( )。
    - Shù zhī yǐng zài húmiàn shàng yáoyè.
    - The shadow of the tree sways on the surface of the lake.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 之](@media/glyph4e4b.png)
### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 時 → 寺 → 寸
- **definition:** inch
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)块(塊)布( )每( )一( )寸( )都( )是( )精( )心( )制(製)作( )。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用( )卷( )尺( )量( )一( )寸( )，每( )一( )寸( )数(數)据(據)都( )准(準)确(確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
- **historical forms:**

### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 候
- **definition:** wait; moment; time; period
- **pinyin:** hòu
- **components:**
  - 亻
    - rén
    - person
  - 侯
    - hóu
    - target for arrows
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 亻 (rén, "person") + 矦(侯) (hóu, ancient form, "target for arrows") =
    - combined human element with phonetic cue from 侯 to imply waiting or time-related activities
  - **interpretation:** The character 候 was designed to convey a sense of humans involved with waiting or being on the lookout, borrowing the sound and visual elements from 侯, which represented a target for arrows, suggesting observation or anticipation.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)稍( )等( )一( )会(會)儿(兒)。
    - Qǐng shāo děng yī huìr.
    - Please wait a moment.
  - 我( )们(們)在( )车(車)站( )等( )候( )，汽( )车(車)却(卻)迟(遲)迟(遲)未( )来(來)。
    - Wǒmen zài chēzhàn děnghòu, qìchē què chíchí wèi lái.
    - We waited at the station, but the bus did not come for a long time.
  - 工作繁忙的候，他( )总(總)是( )很( )疲( )倦( )。
    - Gōngzuò fánmáng de hòu, tā zǒng shì hěn píjuàn.
    - During busy work periods, he always feels tired.
### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 候 → 亻
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Stylization of 人 (rén, "person") as a side radical to depict a person
  - **interpretation:** 亻 is a stylized form of 人 (rén, "person") used to indicate human-related meanings when combined with other components in characters as a radical. It visually represents a standing person, maintaining the core meaning of 'person' while facilitating the construction of complex characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )一( )个(個)热(熱)心( )的( )人( )。
    - Tā shì yī gè rèxīn de rén.
    - He is a kind-hearted person.
  - 这(這)座( )城( )市( )里(裡)住( )着(著)很( )多( )优(優)秀( )的( )人( )。
    - Zhè zuò chéngshì lǐ zhùzhe hěn duō yōuxiù de rén.
    - There are many outstanding people living in this city.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )有( )梦(夢)想( )。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu mèngxiǎng.
    - Everyone has dreams.
### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 候 → 亻 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他( )是( )个(個)好( )人( )。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每( )个(個)人( )都( )有( )责(責)任( )，为(為)社( )会(會)作( )出( )贡(貢)献(獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心( )灵(靈)获(獲)得( )了( )成( )长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.

### 小( )时(時)候( ) → 時候 → 候 → 侯
- **definition:** target for arrows
- **pinyin:** hóu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a target for arrows
  - **interpretation:** The character 侯(hóu, "marquis") originally depicted a target used in archery. This visual connection stems from the idea that a marquis, as a noble rank, could be symbolically associated with such a prestigious or targeted position in society.
- **examples:**
  - 古( )代( )的( )皇( )帝( )会(會)封( )爵( )位( )给(給)侯( )。
    - Gǔdài de huángdì huì fēng juéwèi gěi hóu.
    - In ancient times, emperors would grant titles to marquises.
  - 这(這)个(個)地( )区(區)曾( )经(經)由( )一( )位( )侯( )统(統)治( )。
    - Zhège dìqū céngjīng yóu yī wèi hóu tǒngzhì.
    - This region was once ruled by a marquis.
  - 侯( )爵( )拥(擁)有( )广(廣)阔(闊)的( )领(領)地( )，他( )们(們)的( )权(權)力( )不( )容( )小( )觑(覷)。
    - Hóujué yǒngyǒu guǎngkuò de lǐngdì, tāmen de quánlì bùróng xiǎoqù.
    - Marquises had vast territories, and their power was not to be underestimated.

## 灵(靈)
---
## effective
### líng
---
- **traditional:** 靈
- **definition:** effective
- **pinyin:** líng
- **components:**
  - 霝
    - líng
    - clear, bright weather
  - 巫
    - wū
    - witch
  - 玉
    - yù
    - jade
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 霝 (phonetic) + 玉 (original semantic 'jade') ->
    - later 巫 ('witch') used as semantic in current form ->
    - final form 靈
  - **interpretation:** The character 靈 originally combined a phonetic element with a semantic component that suggested something precious or revered, like 玉(jade). Over time, the semantic component evolved to 巫, associating the character with spirituality or otherworldly power.
  - **simplification:** 靈 was simplified to 灵 by removing the semantic component 巫 and retaining the core phonetic element of 霝.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)药(藥)非( )常( )灵(靈)。
    - Zhège yào fēicháng líng.
    - This medicine is very effective.
  - 他( )的( )方( )法( )真( )灵(靈)！
    - Tā de fāngfǎ zhēn líng!
    - His method is truly effective!
  - 她( )的( )灵(靈)感( )总(總)是( )很( )灵(靈)。
    - Tā de línggǎn zǒngshì hěn líng.
    - Her inspiration is always very effective.
### 灵(靈) → 霝
- **definition:** clear, bright weather
- **pinyin:** líng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts rain with combination of big and small drops
  - **interpretation:** The character 霝(líng) is a pictogram symbolizing the varied sizes of raindrops falling from the sky, capturing a natural scene of rainfall.
### 灵(靈) → 巫
- **definition:** witch
- **pinyin:** wū
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a shaman or witch with ritualistic gestures
  - **interpretation:** The character 巫(wū, 'witch') is traditionally believed to represent a person engaging in shamanic or ritualistic activities, highlighted by the dynamic gestures that suggest the role of a witch or a medium.
- **examples:**
  - 那( )个(個)村( )庄(莊)有( )一( )个(個)著( )名( )的( )巫( )师(師)。
    - Nàge cūnzhuāng yǒu yīgè zhùmíng de wūshī.
    - That village has a famous witch.
  - 传(傳)说(說)中( )，巫( )可( )以( )召( )唤(喚)风(風)雨( )。
    - Chuánshuō zhōng, wū kěyǐ zhàohuàn fēngyǔ.
    - According to legend, the witch can summon storms.
  - 古( )代( )神( )话(話)里(裡)，巫( )常( )常( )与(與)神( )灵(靈)交( )流( )。
    - Gǔdài shénhuà lǐ, wū chángcháng yǔ shénlíng jiāoliú.
    - In ancient myths, witches often communicated with spirits.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 巫](@media/glyph5deb.png)
### 灵(靈) → 玉
- **definition:** jade
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a picture of a cong (琮), a sort of ritual jade totem ->
    - dot added to differentiate from 王 (wáng, "king") ->
    - final form 玉 (yù, "jade")
  - **interpretation:** The character represents a picture of a jade cong, emphasizing its role in rituals and its cultural significance. The image eventually included a distinguishing dot to ensure clarity from similar characters like 王, underscoring the value jade held as a material in ancient contexts.
- **examples:**
  - 她( )收( )到( )了( )一( )个( )漂( )亮( )的( )玉( )手( )镯(鐲)。
    - Tā shōu dào le yī gè piàoliang de yù shǒuzhuó.
    - She received a beautiful jade bracelet.
  - 皇( )帝( )的( )王( )冠( )上( )镶(鑲)嵌( )着(著)闪(閃)耀( )的( )玉( )石( )。
    - Huángdì de wángguān shàng xiāngqiànzhe shǎnyào de yùshí.
    - The emperor's crown was inlaid with shining jade stones.
  - 古( )代( )的( )玉( )器( )常( )常( )被( )视(視)为(為)珍( )贵(貴)的( )艺(藝)术(術)品( )。
    - Gǔdài de yùqì chángcháng bèi shìwéi zhēnguì de yìshùpǐn.
    - Ancient jade artifacts are often regarded as precious works of art.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 玉](@media/glyph7389.png)

## boy; chap; guy
### xiǎozi
---
- **definition:** boy; chap; guy
- **pinyin:** xiǎozi
- **components:**
  - 小
    - xiǎo
    - small; little; young
  - 子
    - zǐ
    - child; son; person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 小 (xiǎo, "small") + 子 (zǐ, "child")
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 小 (xiǎo, "small") and 子 (zǐ, "child") historically signifies a 'small child' or 'boy'. Over time, it has come to be used more broadly to refer to a 'chap' or 'guy' in colloquial contexts, often with a casual or informal tone.
- **examples:**
  - 那( )个(個)小( )子( )总(總)是( )调(調)皮( )捣(搗)蛋( )。
    - Nàge xiǎozi zǒng shì tiáopí dǎodàn.
    - That boy is always being naughty.
  - 这(這)个(個)小( )子( )很( )聪(聰)明( )，学(學)习(習)成( )绩(績)很( )好( )。
    - Zhège xiǎozi hěn cōngmíng, xuéxí chéngjī hěn hǎo.
    - This chap is very smart, and his academic performance is excellent.
  - 那( )个(個)小( )子( )是( )我( )邻(鄰)居( )的( )儿(兒)子( )。
    - Nàge xiǎozi shì wǒ línjū de érzi.
    - That guy is my neighbor's son.
### 小子 → 小
- **definition:** small; little; young
- **pinyin:** xiǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts three small dots arranged symmetrically to represent something small
  - **interpretation:** The character 小(xiǎo, 'small') uses three small strokes to symbolize size or quantity, visually capturing the essence of 'smallness'.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)个(個)小( )猫(貓)很( )可( )爱(愛)。
    - Zhège xiǎo māo hěn kě'ài.

  - **description:** Depicts a baby with a large head and spread arms, with legs wrapped in a blanket
  - **interpretation:** The character 子(zǐ, "child") is a pictorial representation of a baby, emphasizing characteristics like a large head and outstretched arms typical of infants, which conveys the essence of a child. This visual element helps infer its meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)小( )子( )很( )调(調)皮( )。

## 世界
---
## world
### shìjiè
---
- **definition:** world
- **pinyin:** shìjiè
- **components:**
  - 世
    - shì
    - generation; life; era
  - 界
    - jiè
    - boundary; sphere; realm
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 世 (shì, "generation; life; era") refers to the succession of human generations or life stages, encompassing time and overall human existence. 界 (jiè, "boundary; sphere") represents the limits or divisions between different entities or areas, leading to a conception of different realms or domains. Together, they form the idea of the "world" as a sphere consisting of all generations and realms, encompassing all of humankind and the physical domain around them.
  - **interpretation:** 世 (shì, "generation; life; era") emphasizes continuity and the passage of time across human generations, implying a collective human existence over eras. 界 (jiè, "boundary; sphere") is about demarcation, defining spaces or worlds in philosophical, physical, or existential terms. Thus, 世界 (shìjiè) embodies the concept of the world as the overarching domain that includes all human societies and the physical universe in which they exist.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )们(們)住( )在( )一( )个(個)美( )丽(麗)的( )世( )界( )。
    - Wǒmen zhù zài yī gè měilì de shìjiè.
    - We live in a beautiful world.
  - 世界上有很多不同的文化。
    - Shìjiè shàng yǒu hěn duō bùtóng de wénhuà.
    - There are many different cultures in the world.
  - 科( )学(學)家( )在( )探( )索( )新( )的( )世( )界( )。
    - Kēxuéjiā zài tànsuǒ xīn de shìjiè.
    - Scientists are exploring new worlds.
### 世界 → 世
- **definition:** generation; life; era
- **pinyin:** shì
- **components:**
  - 枼
    - yè
    - leaf
  - 葉
    - yè
    - leaf
  - 十
    - shí
    - ten
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** jiajie
  - **description:**
    - Variant form of 枼 (original form of 葉) with the tree removed ->
    - borrowed meaning for 'generation'; traditionally explained as triplicated 十 ('thirty'), referencing thirty years as a standard generation ->
    - simplified to adopt new meaning
  - **interpretation:** The character 世 originated as a variant of 枼, the word for 'leaf', with the tree component removed, representing a borrowing of its shape for the phonetic similarity. Over time, it acquired a meaning related to 'generation' due to the interpretation of triplicated 十, symbolizing a traditional thirty-year generation cycle, which is how it came to represent age or lifetime.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)一( )代( )人( )肩( )负(負)着(著)重( )大( )的( )责(責)任( )。
    - Zhè yī dài rén jiānfùzhe zhòngdà de zérèn.
    - This generation shoulders a great responsibility.
  - 他( )用( )一( )生( )的( )努( )力( )创(創)造( )了( )伟(偉)大( )的( )成( )就( )。
    - Tā yòng yī shēng de nǔlì chuàngzàole wěidà de chéngjiù.
    - He used a lifetime of effort to create great achievements.
  - 整( )个(個)世( )纪(紀)的( )历(歷)史( )都( )记(記)载(載)在( )这(這)本( )书(書)里(裡)。
    - Zhěnggè shìjì de lìshǐ dōu jìzǎi zài zhè běn shū lǐ.
    - The history of the entire century is recorded in this book.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 世](@media/glyph4e16.png)
### 世界 → 世 → 枼
- **definition:** leaf
- **pinyin:** yè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts leaves growing from a tree (original form of 葉 (yè, "leaf"))
  - **interpretation:** Depicts leaves on a branch, representing both the specific physical forms of 'leaf' as well as the larger conceptual category of things that are flat like leaves. This intuitive extension made it a fitting choice to also represent the concept of 'flat' due to the physical characteristic of flatness associated with leaves.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 枼](@media/glyph67bc.png)
### 世界 → 世 → 葉
- **definition:** leaf
- **pinyin:** yè
- **components:**
  - 艸
    - cǎo
    - grass; plant
  - 枼
    - yè
    - leaf
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艸 (cǎo, "grass; plant") + phonetic 枼 (yè, "leaf") ->
    - depiction of a leaf
  - **interpretation:** The character 葉(yè, "leaf") is formed by combining 艸 (cǎo, "grass; plant") as the semantic component, representing its association with plants, with 枼 (yè, "leaf") as the phonetic component conveying the pronunciation. This results in the character meaning 'leaf,' representing the part of a plant.
  - **simplification:** In the simplified version 叶(葉), the semantic 艸 (cǎo, "grass; plant") is removed while retaining the phonetic 十, maintaining the connection to the sound but with fewer strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 秋天到了，树(樹)上( )的( )叶(葉)子( )变(變)黄(黃)了( )。
    - Qiūtiān dàole, shù shàng de yèzi biàn huáng le.
    - Autumn has arrived, and the leaves on the trees have turned yellow.
  - 一( )片( )叶(葉)子( )飘(飄)落( )在( )地( )上( )。
    - Yí piàn yèzi piāoluò zài dì shàng.
    - A leaf drifted down to the ground.
  - 风(風)吹( )过(過)时(時)，树(樹)叶(葉)沙( )沙( )作( )响(響)。
    - Fēng chuīguò shí, shùyè shāshā zuòxiǎng.
    - When the wind blows, the leaves rustle.
### 世界 → 世 → 葉 → 艸
- **definition:** grass; plant
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - grass
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts grass blades ->
    - duplication of 屮 (chè, 'grass') ->
    - grass imagery
  - **interpretation:** The character 艸(cǎo, 'grass') is a pictorial representation of grass blades. It is essentially a duplication of the character 屮 (chè, 'grass'), visually suggesting the appearance of grass tufts through repetition, emphasizing the concept of grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 公( )园(園)里(裡)绿(綠)艸( )茵( )茵( )。

    - The morning dew nourishes the cluster of grass, and the breeze makes them dance.
  - 秋( )天( )时(時)艸( )变(變)黄(黃)，冬天它又枯萎。

  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**

### 世界 → 世 → 十
- **definition:** ten
- **pinyin:** shí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original vertical stroke ->
    - later horizontal stroke added ->
    - forms a cross ->
    - represents 'ten'
  - **interpretation:** The character 十(shí, 'ten') represents the number ten with a cross shape that could be seen as tally marks. It evolved from a simple vertical stroke to a cross by adding a horizontal stroke, symbolizing a complete set of ten.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )有( )十( )本( )书(書)。
    - Wǒ yǒu shí běn shū.
    - I have ten books.

    - boundary; realm
  - **interpretation:** The character 界 (jiè, "boundary; realm") combines 田 (tián, "field") as the semantic component and 介 (jiè) as the phonetic component. Fields often have boundaries, and this association naturally leads to the concept of 'boundary' which is essential in defining realms or territories.

### 世界 → 界 → 介
- **definition:** to mediate
- **pinyin:** jiè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a person standing between two lines or boundaries
  - **interpretation:** The character 介 (jiè, 'to derive an idea from') represents the concept of being in-between or acting as a mediator. It conceptually fits the idea of deriving by positioning oneself between different ideas or entities.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )从(從)古( )代( )诗(詩)词(詞)中( )介( )出( )艺(藝)术(術)灵(靈)感( )。
    - Tā cóng gǔdài shīcí zhōng jiè chū yìshù línggǎn.
    - He derives artistic inspiration from ancient poems.
  - 科( )学(學)家( )阅(閱)读(讀)文( )献(獻)时(時)介( )出( )创(創)新( )思( )想( )，工( )程( )师(師)从(從)实(實)验(驗)结(結)果( )中( )介( )出( )改( )进(進)方( )案( )。
    - Kēxuéjiā yuèdú wénxiàn shí jiè chū chuàngxīn sīxiǎng, gōngchéngshī cóng shíyàn jiéguǒ zhōng jiè chū gǎijìn fāng'àn.
    - Scientists derive innovative ideas when reading literature, and engineers derive improvement plans from experimental results.
  - 研( )究( )者( )从(從)历(歷)史( )资(資)料( )中( )介( )出( )重( )要( )信(資)息(訊)。

## 埃及
---
## Egypt
### Āijí
---
- **definition:** Egypt
- **pinyin:** Āijí
- **components:**
  - 埃
    - āi
    - dust; angstrom
  - 及
    - jí
    - and; to reach; up to
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** The word 埃及 (āijí, "Egypt") combines two characters that individually don't convey its modern meaning as a country name, but together they represent the ancient nation of Egypt. As with many foreign place names transliterated into Chinese, the characters were chosen for their phonetic resemblance rather than meaning.
  - **interpretation:** The word 埃及 (āijí, "Egypt") is a phonetic transcription rather than a semantic one. It does not relate to any specific attributes of Egypt but provides a sound approximation using available Chinese characters.
- **examples:**
  - 我打算去埃及旅行。
    - Wǒ dǎsuàn qù Āijí lǚxíng.
    - I plan to travel to Egypt.
  - 埃及的金字塔非常著名。
    - Āijí de jīnzìtǎ fēicháng zhùmíng.
    - The pyramids of Egypt are very famous.
  - 去年夏天，我( )们(們)去( )了( )埃( )及( )和( )希( )腊(臘)。
    - Qùnián xiàtiān, wǒmen qùle Āijí hé Xīlà.
    - Last summer, we went to Egypt and Greece.
### 埃及 → 埃
- **definition:** dust; angstrom
- **pinyin:** āi
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth; soil
  - 矣
    - yǐ
    - final particle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 土 (tǔ, "earth; soil") + phonetic 矣 (yǐ) ->
    - dust
  - **interpretation:** The character 埃 combines the semantic element 土 (tǔ, "earth; soil"), indicating a connection to earth or material substances, with 矣 (yǐ) as the phonetic component, which does not carry meaning here but provides the pronunciation. The meaning 'dust' relates directly to fine particles originating from soil or ground.
- **examples:**
  - 房( )间(間)里(裡)满(滿)是( )灰( )尘(塵)，桌( )子( )上( )覆( )盖(蓋)了( )一( )层(層)厚( )厚( )的( )埃( )。
    - Fángjiān lǐ mǎn shì huīchén，zhuōzi shàng fùgài le yī céng hòuhòu de āi.
    - The room is full of dust, and the table is covered with a thick layer of dust.
  - 在( )显(顯)微( )镜(鏡)下( )，我( )们(們)可( )以( )看( )到( )每( )一( )个(個)埃( )的( )细(細)节(節)。
    - Zài xiǎnwēijìng xià，wǒmen kěyǐ kàn dào měi yī gè āi de xìjié.
    - Under the microscope, we can see the details of each angstrom.
### 埃及 → 埃 → 土
- **definition:** earth; soil
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民( )耕( )土( )，种(種)出( )丰(豐)收( )。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院( )子( )里(裡)的( )土( )，适(適)合( )种(種)花( )。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 土](@media/glyph571f.png)
### 埃及 → 埃 → 矣
- **definition:** final particle
- **pinyin:** yǐ
- **components:**
  - 矢
    - shǐ
    - arrow
  - 㠯
    - yǐ
    - use, take
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 矢 (shǐ, "arrow") + phonetic 㠯 ->
    - particle indicating completed action
  - **interpretation:** 矢 (shǐ, "arrow") is used as a semantic guide, suggesting a sense of direction or completion, while 㠯 provides the phonetic contribution. Together, they form a particle used to indicate the completion of an action or a finalized state.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )终(終)於( )到( )达(達)目( )的( )地( )矣( )。
    - Wǒ zhōngyú dàodá mùdìdì yǐ.
    - I have finally reached the destination.
  - 一切皆已成矣。
    - Yīqiè jiē yǐ chéng yǐ.
    - Everything has been accomplished.
  - 他( )离(離)开(開)多( )时(時)矣( )。

    - He has been gone for a long time.

  - 他( )拉( )开(開)弓( )，射出一支矢。

### 埃及 → 埃 → 矣 → 㠯
- **definition:** use, take
- **pinyin:** yǐ
- **components:**
  - 耜
    - sì
    - plow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally depicted a plow ->
    - Related to the original form of 耜 (sì, "plow")
  - **interpretation:** The character 㠯 originally depicted a plow, providing insight into early agricultural tools and practices. It served as the original form for 耜 (sì, "plow"), reflecting its functional purpose in farming.
### 埃及 → 埃 → 矣 → 㠯 → 耜
- **definition:** plow
- **pinyin:** sì
- **components:**
  - 耒
    - lěi
    - plow
  - 㠯
    - use, take
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:** semantic 耒 (lěi, "plow") + phonetic 㠯
  - **interpretation:** The character 耜(sì, "plow") combines the semantic component 耒 (lěi, "plow"), representing the agricultural tool, with the phonetic component 㠯 to convey the sound. The semantic component indicates its association with farming and plowing, while the phonetic element suggests the pronunciation.
### 埃及 → 埃 → 矣 → 㠯 → 耜 → 耒
- **definition:** plow
- **pinyin:** lěi
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a wooden bifurcated plow with originally three cross lines (彡 and 丯) for plow furrows ->
    - later simplified to two cross lines ->
    - final form 耒
  - **interpretation:** The character 耒 (lěi, 'tilling tool') directly represents an ancient agricultural implement, visually illustrating its structure with the cross lines symbolizing furrows made by the tool. This clearly links the character's shape to its function in farming.

### 埃及 → 及
- **definition:** and; to reach; up to
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 又 (yòu, "hand") =
    - a hand grabbing a person ->
    - to reach
  - **interpretation:** The character 及(jí, "and; to reach") combines 人 (rén, "person") with 又 (yòu, "hand") to depict the idea of a hand catching up to or reaching for a person. This visual metaphor effectively communicates the concept of reaching or arriving at something.
- **examples:**

  - 我( )们(們)可( )以( )提( )供( )餐( )饮(飲)及( )住( )宿( )服( )务(務)。
