## 地( )图(圖)
---
## map; plat; atlas
### dìtú
---
- **traditional:** 地圖
- **definition:** map; plat; atlas
- **pinyin:** dìtú
- **components:**
  - 地
    - dì
    - earth; ground; land; place
  - 图(圖)
    - tú
    - diagram; picture; drawing; map
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** In the word 地( )图(圖) (dìtú, "map"), 地 (dì, "earth; ground") refers to the land or ground, and 圖 (tú, "diagram; picture") refers to a drawing or diagram. Together, these characters are used to describe a diagram or representation of a section of the earth's surface or ground, which is essentially what a map is.
  - **interpretation:** A 地( )圖(图) (dìtú, "map") is a representation or diagram of the earth's surface, which fits logically with its components: 地 (dì, "earth") and 圖 (tú, "diagram").
- **examples:**
  - 他( )给(給)我( )看( )了( )一( )张(張)地( )图(圖)。
    - Tā gěi wǒ kàn le yī zhāng dìtú.
    - He showed me a map.
  - 我( )在( )寻(尋)找( )图(圖)书(書)馆(館)的( )位( )置( )，但( )地( )图(圖)不( )是( )很( )清( )晰( )。
    - Wǒ zài xúnzhǎo túshūguǎn de wèizhì, dàn dìtú bù shì hěn qīngxī.
    - I am looking for the library's location, but the map is not very clear.
  - 这(這)本( )书(書)包( )含( )了( )世( )界( )各( )地( )的( )地( )图(圖)。
    - Zhè běn shū bāohán le shìjiè gèdì de dìtú.
    - This book contains maps of various places around the world.
### 地( )图(圖) → 地
- **definition:** earth; ground; land; place
- **pinyin:** dì
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
  - 也
    - yě
    - also
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 土 (tǔ, "earth") + phonetic 也 (yě) ->
    - earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 地 (dì, "earth") combines the semantic element 土 (tǔ, "earth") suggesting the concept of ground or soil, with the phonetic element 也 (yě) providing the sound. This construction intuitively links the meaning of earth or ground with its pronunciation.
- **examples:**
  - 小( )狗( )在( )地( )上( )打( )滚(滾)。
    - Xiǎo gǒu zài dì shàng dǎgǔn.
    - The puppy is rolling on the ground.
  - 地( )震( )后(後)，居( )民( )们(們)迅( )速( )疏( )散( )。
    - Dìzhèn hòu, jūmín men xùnsù shūsàn.
    - After the earthquake, the residents quickly evacuated.
  - 农(農)民( )们(們)正( )在( )田( )地( )里(裡)工( )作( )。
    - Nóngmín men zhèngzài tiándì lǐ gōngzuò.

### 地( )图(圖) → 地 → 也

  - **description:** Depicts a forked object or footprint
  - **interpretation:** The character 也 (yě, "also") is a pictogram that originally depicted a forked object or possibly a footprint. It does not represent a specific entity but evolved to be used phonemically, contributing its sound to form other characters.

### 地( )图(圖) → 图(圖)
- **traditional:** 圖
- **definition:** diagram; picture; drawing; map
- **pinyin:** tú
- **components:**
  - 囧
    - jiǒng
    - window
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic: 囧 (jiǒng, "window") + semantic: 口 (kǒu, "mouth") =
    - a picture drawn within a boundary ->
    - picture/map
  - **interpretation:** The character 图 (tú) combines 囧 (jiǒng, "window") as the phonetic element, suggesting a rectangular shape like a window or a frame, with 口 (kǒu, "mouth") as a semantic component, indicating an enclosed area, apt for depicting enclosed spaces like a map or diagram.
  - **simplification:** 圖 → 图: Simplified by removing the inner complexity of 囧 and representing the frame with a simpler structure, retaining the outer 口 for consistency.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)幅( )图(圖)展( )示( )了( )城( )市( )历(歷)史( )。
    - Zhè fú tú zhǎnshì le chéngshì lìshǐ.
    - This picture displays the city's history.
  - 我( )根( )据(據)图(圖)来(來)规(規)划(劃)路( )线(線)，并(並)成( )功( )到( )达(達)目( )的( )地( )。
    - Wǒ gēnjù tú lái guīhuà lùxiàn, bìng chénggōng dàodá mùdìdì.
    - I used the map to plan the route and successfully reached my destination.
  - 他( )绘(繪)制(製)了( )一( )张(張)图(圖)，记(記)录(錄)了( )人( )生( )旅( )程( )。
    - Tā huìzhì le yī zhāng tú, jìlù le rénshēng lǚchéng.
    - He drew a picture to document his life journey.
### 地( )图(圖) → 图(圖) → 囧
- **definition:** window
- **pinyin:** jiǒng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a window with an open lattice pattern
  - **interpretation:** The character 囧(jǒng, "window") originally represents a window with an open lattice design, illustrating its functional purpose as a framework for ventilation and light.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)扇( )囧( )很( )大( )。
    - Zhè shàn jiǒng hěn dà.
    - This window is very large.
  - 早( )晨( )透( )过(過)囧( )射( )进(進)温(溫)暖( )的( )光( )，一( )切( )焕(煥)然( )一( )新( )。
    - Zǎochén tòuguò jiǒng shè jìn wēnnuǎn de guāng, yīqiè huànrán yīxīn.
    - In the morning, warm light poured in through the window, and everything looked brand new.
  - 老( )屋( )的( )囧( )保( )存( )着(著)历(歷)史( )的( )痕( )迹(跡)，诉(訴)说(說)着(著)往( )昔( )的( )故( )事( )。
    - Lǎowū de jiǒng bǎocún zhe lìshǐ de hénjì, sùshuō zhe wǎngxī de gùshì.
    - The old house's window preserves traces of history and tells stories of the past.
- **historical forms:**

### 地( )图(圖) → 图(圖) → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )张(張)开(開)口( )，大( )声(聲)喊( )叫( )。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口( )饭(飯)入( )口( )即( )化( )。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小( )女( )孩( )咬( )了( )一( )口( )苹(蘋)果( )，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
- **historical forms:**

## 轮(輪)
---
## take turns
### lún
---
- **traditional:** 輪
- **definition:** take turns
- **pinyin:** lún
- **components:**
  - 車
    - chē
    - carriage
  - 侖
    - lún
    - order
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 車 (chē, "carriage") + phonetic 侖 (lún, "order") ->
    - take turns
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 車 (chē, "carriage"), indicating the wheel's association with vehicles, and 侖 (lún, "order"), suggesting the orderly sequence or turning. This imagery of a wheel turning in an orderly fashion leads to the idea of 'taking turns'.
  - **simplification:** The traditional form 輪 was simplified by replacing 車 (chē, "carriage") with 车, and 侖 (lún, "order") with 仑, reducing the character's complexity while preserving both the semantic vehicle and the sound.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )们(們)应(應)该(該)轮(輪)流( )洗( )碗( )。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi lúnliú xǐwǎn.
    - We should take turns washing the dishes.
  - 老( )师(師)让(讓)每( )个(個)学(學)生( )轮(輪)流( )发(發)言( )。
    - Lǎoshī ràng měi gè xuéshēng lúnliú fāyán.
    - The teacher asked each student to take turns speaking.
  - 在( )晚( )会(會)上( )，他( )们(們)轮(輪)流( )表( )演( )节(節)目( )。
    - Zài wǎnhuì shàng, tāmen lúnliú biǎoyǎn jiémù.
    - At the party, they took turns performing.
### 轮(輪) → 車
- **definition:** carriage
- **pinyin:** chē
- **components:**
  - 田
    - tián
    - field
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a carriage viewed from above; wheels on both sides + sun shade on top ->
    - depicted vertically with wheels as strokes and loading area marked by 田 (tián, "field") ->
    - 車
  - **interpretation:** The character 車(chē, "vehicle") originally depicts a carriage from an overhead perspective. The transformation into the vertical form involved simplifying the depiction of wheels and emphasizing the loading area, marked by a field symbol, creating a streamlined pictographic representation.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 車 was simplified to 车 by reducing the number of strokes, maintaining the overall shape of the vehicle but removing intricate details.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )坐( )车(車)去( )上( )班( )。
    - Wǒ zuò chē qù shàngbān.
    - I take a car to go to work.
  - 这(這)辆(輛)车(車)很( )快( )。
    - Zhè liàng chē hěn kuài.
    - This car is very fast.
  - 我( )想( )买(買)一( )辆(輛)新( )车(車)。
    - Wǒ xiǎng mǎi yī liàng xīn chē.
    - I want to buy a new car.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 車](@media/glyph8eca.png)
### 轮(輪) → 車 → 田
- **definition:** field
- **pinyin:** tián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a field divided into four sections
  - **interpretation:** The character 田(tián, 'field') visually represents a field with sections, indicating its agricultural use and importance in ancient times.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民( )在( )田( )里(裡)耕( )作( )。
    - Nóngmín zài tián lǐ gēngzuò.
    - The farmer works in the field.
  - 那( )边(邊)的( )田( )长(長)满(滿)了( )庄(莊)稼( )，农(農)民( )收( )获(穫)忙( )碌( )。
    - Nàbiān de tián cháng mǎn le zhuāngjià, nóngmín shōuhuò mánglù.
    - The field over there is full of crops, and the farmer is busy harvesting.
  - 秋( )收( )时(時)节(節)，人( )们(們)忙( )于(於)收( )割( )田( )里(裡)的( )稻( )谷( )。
    - Qiūshōu shíjié, rénmen máng yú shōugē tián lǐ de dàogǔ.
    - During the harvest season, people are busy reaping the rice in the fields.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 田](@media/glyph7530.png)
### 轮(輪) → 侖
- **definition:** order
- **pinyin:** lún
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jí
    - gather
  - 冊
    - cè
    - book
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 亼 (gather, or mouth) + 冊 (book) =
    - gathering books or reading aloud ->
    - meaning related to order or logic
  - **interpretation:** The character 侖(lún) combines 亼, which can symbolize gathering or a mouth speaking, with 冊, meaning 'book', to depict an action associated with organizing or arranging books, ultimately indicating order or coherence.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 侖](@media/glyph4f96.png)
### 轮(輪) → 侖 → 亼
- **definition:** gather
- **pinyin:** jí
- **components:**
  - 入
    - rù
    - enter
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
  - 今
    - jīn
    - now
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gathering from three sides ->
    - original form of 今 (jīn, "now")
  - **interpretation:** 亼 (jī, "open mouth flipped upside down") originally represented the action of gathering, with 入 (rù, "enter") suggesting bringing things together and 一 (yī, "one") implying unification into a single entity. This concept aligns traditionally with 集 (jí, "gather"), where the sense of gathering from three sides connects to assembling or coming together. The visual comparison to an open mouth reversed is a less common interpretation, relating to a shape rather than function.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 亼](@media/glyph4ebc.png)

  - **description:** An arrowhead indicating 'to enter'

### 轮(輪) → 侖 → 亼 → 今
- **definition:** now
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **components:**
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - to speak
  - 亼
    - jí
    - collect; assemble
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 曰 (yuē, "to speak") inverted with 亼-like structure + horizontal stroke ->
    - original form implying 'not to speak' or 'keep in mouth'
  - **interpretation:** The character depicts an inverted version of 曰 (yuē, "to speak"), with a structure resembling 亼 and a horizontal stroke, representing something placed in the mouth, leading to the sense of 'keeping in the mouth' or 'not speaking'. This image of being contained or holding leads to 'now', as in holding or having the present moment.
- **examples:**
  - 今( )天( )的( )天( )气(氣)不( )错(錯)。
    - Jīntiān de tiānqì bùcuò.
    - Today's weather is nice.
  - 现(現)在( )是( )吃( )晚( )饭(飯)的( )时(時)候( )。
    - Xiànzài shì chī wǎnfàn de shíhòu.
    - Now is the time to have dinner.
  - 她( )今( )天( )特( )别(別)忙( )，没(沒)时(時)间(間)见(見)面( )。
    - Tā jīntiān tèbié máng, méi shíjiān jiànmiàn.
    - She is especially busy today and doesn't have time to meet.
### 轮(輪) → 侖 → 亼 → 今 → 曰
- **definition:** to speak
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老( )师(師)曰( )：勤( )奋(奮)是( )成( )功( )之( )母( )。

    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'

    - books; documents
  - **interpretation:** The character 冊(cè, 'a form made by lining up pieces of wood and binding them together') represents bamboo slips tied together with string, symbolizing early forms of books or documents compiled in this manner.
  - **simplification:** 冊 was simplified to 册 by removing interior strokes, forming a more straightforward and less intricate version.

## 烧(燒)
---
## boil; burn
### shāo
---
- **traditional:** 燒
- **definition:** boil; burn
- **pinyin:** shāo
- **components:**
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
  - 堯
    - yáo
    - a legendary emperor; tall
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 火 (huǒ, "fire") + phonetic 堯 (yáo, "a legendary emperor; tall") ->
    - boil; burn
  - **interpretation:** 火 (huǒ, 'fire') is involved with ignition or heating -> burning -> when combined with 堯 (yáo), which contributes the sound, the character represents the action of boiling or burning where fire is a primary element in producing heat.
  - **simplification:** 燒 was simplified to 烧 by replacing the 呪 (zhòu, "curse") [incorrect as listed] radical 堯 (yáo, "a legendary emperor; tall") with its simplified version 尧.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)帮(幫)我( )把( )水( )烧(燒)开(開)。
    - Qǐng bāng wǒ bǎ shuǐ shāo kāi.
    - Please help me boil the water.
  - 他( )不( )小( )心( )把( )手( )指( )烧(燒)伤(傷)了( )。
    - Tā bù xiǎo xīn bǎ shǒu zhǐ shāo shāng le.
    - He accidentally burned his finger.
  - 这(這)道( )菜( )需( )要( )烧(燒)很( )长(長)时(時)间(間)。
    - Zhè dào cài xū yào shāo hěn cháng shí jiān.
    - This dish needs to be cooked for a long time.
### 烧(燒) → 火
- **definition:** fire
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火( )在( )壁( )炉(爐)中( )熊( )熊( )燃( )烧(燒)。
    - Huǒ zài bìlú zhōng xióngxióng ránshāo.
    - The fire burns fiercely in the fireplace.
  - 野( )外( )露( )营(營)时(時)，火( )能( )驱(驅)走( )寒( )冷( )。
    - Yěwài lùyíng shí, huǒ néng qūzǒu hánlěng.
    - When camping outdoors, the fire can drive away the cold.
  - 遇( )到( )火( )灾(災)时(時)，迅( )速( )疏( )散( )最( )为(為)重( )要( )。
    - Yù dào huǒzāi shí, xùnsù shū sàn zuìwéi zhòngyào.
    - In case of a fire, evacuating quickly is of utmost importance.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 火](@media/glyph706b.png)
### 烧(燒) → 堯
- **definition:** a legendary emperor; tall
- **pinyin:** yáo
- **components:**
  - 垚
    - yáo
    - tall (of earth)
  - 兀
    - wù
    - towering and bald
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound and ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic 垚 (earth layers, *ŋeːw) + semantic 兀 (towering and bald) ->
    - Depicts tall earth + kneeling man =
    - legendary ruler
  - **interpretation:** The character 堯 (yáo) combines phonetic 垚, which represents layers of earth and sounds like *ŋeːw, with semantic 兀, depicting a towering and bald figure. This combination suggests a legendary ruler who stands tall like the earth and exhibits a commanding presence. Such a ruler is perceived as lofty and powerful, akin to the towering formation of earth.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 堯](@media/glyph582f.png)
### 烧(燒) → 堯 → 垚
- **definition:** tall (of earth)
- **pinyin:** yáo
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 垚 (triplication of 土 (tǔ, "earth") =
    - "tall (of earth)"
  - **interpretation:** 垚 is an ideogrammic compound composed of three 土 (tǔ, "earth") characters stacked together, symbolizing a mound or a tall accumulation of earth. This character uses repetition to emphasize the abundance or height of the soil, representing the concept of 'tall'.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 垚](@media/glyph579a.png)
### 烧(燒) → 堯 → 垚 → 土
- **definition:** earth
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民( )耕( )土( )，种(種)出( )丰(豐)收( )。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院( )子( )里(裡)的( )土( )，适(適)合( )种(種)花( )。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 土](@media/glyph571f.png)
### 烧(燒) → 堯 → 兀
- **definition:** towering and bald
- **pinyin:** wù
- **components:**
  - 尢
    - wān
    - man with bent legs
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant form
  - **description:** 兀 is a variant form of 尢 (wān, "man with bent legs")
  - **interpretation:** 兀 originally represented a man with bent legs, indicative of jumping or collapsing. It connects to this meaning by representing something that stands out or is elevated, as in 'towering.' It reflects the semantic notion of standing out both physically and metaphorically.
- **examples:**
  - 那座山峰兀立，宛如巨人昂首。
    - Nà zuò shānfēng wùlì, wǎnrú jùrén ángshǒu.
    - That mountain peak towers, like a giant with its head held high.
  - 古( )树(樹)枝( )干(幹)兀( )然( )裸( )露( )，诉(訴)说(說)着(著)岁(歲)月( )沧(滄)桑( )。
    - Gǔ shù zhīgàn wùrán luǒlù, sùshuōzhe suìyuè cāngsāng.
    - The ancient tree's branches stand bald and exposed, telling tales of time’s vicissitudes.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 兀](@media/glyph5140.png)
### 烧(燒) → 堯 → 兀 → 尢
- **definition:** man with bent legs
- **pinyin:** wān
- **components:**
  - 尤
    - yóu
    - especially
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant form of 尢
  - **description:**
    - Pictogram: Originally depicts a hand with a wart ->
    - Variant form of 尤: retaining connotations of deformity
  - **interpretation:** 尢 is identified as a variant of 尤 and represents the notion of a man with bent legs, closely associating with deformity or deviation in form. The character still conveys variations perceived as abnormalities, similar to the original meaning of a hand with a wart.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )行( )走( )时(時)显(顯)露( )出( )尢( )样(樣)步( )态(態)，引( )得( )众(眾)人( )侧(側)目( )。
    - tā xíngzǒu shí xiǎnlù chū wān yàng bùtài, yǐn dé zhòngrén cèmù.
    - When he walked, his bent-legged gait was evident, attracting sidelong glances from the crowd.
  - 古( )籍( )记(記)载(載)尢( )人( )的( )形( )态(態)。
    - gǔjí jìzǎi wān rén de xíngtài.
    - Ancient texts record the appearance of a man with bent legs.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 尢](@media/glyph5c22.png)
### 烧(燒) → 堯 → 兀 → 尢 → 尤
- **definition:** especially
- **pinyin:** yóu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand with a wart ->
    - Original form of 疣 (yóu, "wart") and 肬(躍) (yóu, "elevated")
  - **interpretation:** 尤 (yóu, "hand with a wart") is a pictogram that initially represented the image of a hand marked by a wart. It served as the original form for characters related to irregularities like 疣 (yóu, "wart").
- **examples:**
  - 医(醫)生( )检(檢)查( )时(時)发(發)现(現)他( )左( )手( )有( )一( )块(塊)尤( )，需( )及( )时(時)治( )疗(療)。
    - Yīshēng jiǎnchá shí fāxiàn tā zuǒshǒu yǒu yí kuài yóu, xū jíshí zhìliáo.
    - During the examination, the doctor discovered that his left hand had a wart and needed prompt treatment.
  - 古( )人( )检(檢)测(測)身( )相( )时(時)，会(會)观(觀)察( )是( )否( )有( )尤( )。
    - Gǔ rén jiǎncè shēnxiàng shí, huì guānchá shìfǒu yǒu yóu.
    - In ancient physiognomy, people would observe whether a hand with a wart was present.

## 洗澡
---
## have a bath
### xǐzǎo
---
- **definition:** have a bath
- **pinyin:** xǐzǎo
- **components:**
  - 洗
    - xǐ
    - wash
  - 澡
    - zǎo
    - bath
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 洗 (xǐ, "wash") refers to the act of cleansing, typically involving water. 澡 (zǎo, "bath") indicates a soaking process to cleanse the body. The combination implies the action of having a bath or a thorough wash.
  - **interpretation:** 洗 (xǐ, "wash") involves the action of cleansing by scrubbing or rinsing. 澡 (zǎo, "bath") suggests the traditional method of immersing oneself in water for purification or relaxation. Together, 洗澡 (xǐzǎo, "have a bath") conveys the act of immersing in water and washing away dirt, thereby achieving cleanliness.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )每( )天( )睡( )觉(覺)之( )前( )都( )会(會)洗( )澡( )。
    - Wǒ měitiān shuìjiào zhīqián dōu huì xǐzǎo.
    - I have a bath every day before going to bed.
  - 他( )在( )运(運)动(動)后(後)马(馬)上( )去( )洗( )澡( )。
    - Tā zài yùndòng hòu mǎshàng qù xǐzǎo.
    - He goes to have a bath immediately after exercising.
  - 小( )王( )喜( )欢(歡)用( )热(熱)水( )洗( )澡( )。
    - Xiǎo Wáng xǐhuān yòng rèshuǐ xǐzǎo.
    - Xiao Wang likes to have a bath with hot water.
### 洗澡 → 洗
- **definition:** wash
- **pinyin:** xǐ
- **components:**
  - 水
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 先
    - xiān
    - before
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 水 (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic 先 (xiān) ->
    - wash
  - **interpretation:** The character 洗(xǐ, "wash") combines the semantic component 水 (shuǐ, "water"), indicating the involvement of water in the action, with the phonetic component 先 (xiān), which provides the pronunciation. This pairing effectively conveys the meaning of washing or cleaning, which naturally involves water.
- **examples:**
  - 我洗了碗。
    - Wǒ xǐle wǎn.
    - I washed the dishes.
  - 她每天洗衣服，所( )以( )总(總)是( )很( )忙( )。

    - Tā yòng rèshuǐ xǐ liǎn.
    - He washes his face with hot water.
### 洗澡 → 洗 → 水

- **pinyin:** shuǐ

  - **interpretation:** 水 (shuǐ, 'water') is a pictogram that directly represents the appearance of flowing water, making it intuitive and easy to recognize. Its simplicity and direct visual reference to its meaning have allowed it to remain unchanged over millennia.
- **examples:**
  - 水( )是( )一( )种(種)生( )命( )之( )源( )。

### 洗澡 → 洗 → 先
- **definition:** before
- **pinyin:** xiān
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 儿
    - ér
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 止 (zhǐ, "foot") + 儿 (ér, "person") =
    - foot in front of person ->
    - to go forward ->
    - first, previous
  - **interpretation:** The character 先(xiān, "first; previous") combines 止 (zhǐ, "foot") and 儿 (ér, "person") to depict a foot moving forward in front of a person, symbolizing the act of proceeding or being ahead, leading to the meaning of 'first' as something that goes before or precedes others.
- **examples:**
  - 我先去商店。
    - Wǒ xiān qù shāngdiàn.
    - I will go to the store first.
  - 你( )需( )要( )先( )完( )成( )作( )业(業)，然( )后(後)才( )能( )看( )电(電)视(視)。
    - Nǐ xūyào xiān wánchéng zuòyè, ránhòu cáinéng kàn diànshì.
    - You need to finish your homework first, then you can watch TV.
  - 请(請)先( )听(聽)我( )说(說)，再( )决(決)定( )。
    - Qǐng xiān tīng wǒ shuō, zài juédìng.
    - Please listen to me first before making a decision.

### 洗澡 → 洗 → 先 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)的( )止( )需( )要( )静(靜)养(養)。

### 洗澡 → 洗 → 先 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - halt
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 止 (zhǐ) ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating the general area involved, with 止 (zhǐ) providing the sound and potentially suggesting the idea of a part of the foot that 'halts' or 'stops' progression, which naturally leads to the notion of a toe.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )脚(腳)趾( )受( )伤(傷)了( )。

### 洗澡 → 洗 → 先 → 止 → 趾 → 足

    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'

### 洗澡 → 洗 → 先 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized footprint pointing upward ->
    - originally meaning 'foot' ->
    - later forms like 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') refer back to original meaning
  - **interpretation:** 龰 (yù, 'stylized feet') is a pictogram showing a footprint pointing up, originally indicating the concept of a foot. The character 趾 (zhǐ, 'toe') evolved from this and retains the reference to the original meaning. It visually resembles a sole with three toes, similar to representations of the human hand in characters like 爪 (zhuǎ, 'claw'), 寸 (cùn, 'inch'), and 又 (yòu, 'again').
### 洗澡 → 洗 → 先 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )用( )手( )写(寫)字( )。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈(媽)妈(媽)牵(牽)着(著)我( )的( )手( )走( )路( )。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他( )的( )手( )很( )温(溫)暖( )，带(帶)给(給)我( )力( )量( )。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.

  - **interpretation:** The character 兒 (ér, "child") is a pictogram representing a child with a distinctive fontanelle, highlighting the child's young age and the characteristic soft spot on the head. This reflects the character's meaning as 'child.'
  - **simplification:** 儿 is a simplified and cursive form of 兒, representing a stylistic reduction of strokes while still retaining the essence of a child's figure.
- **examples:**

### 洗澡 → 澡 → 喿 → 品

## 洗澡

## 围(圍)
---
## wrap; swathe
### wéi
---
- **traditional:** 圍
- **definition:** wrap; swathe
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 囗
    - wéi
    - enclosure
  - 韋
    - wéi
    - soft leather
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 囗 (wéi, "enclosure") + 韋 (wéi, "soft leather") =
    - something surrounded by an enclosure ->
    - surround
  - **interpretation:** The character 围(圍) (wéi, "surround") combines the concept of an enclosure with the phonetic element 韋 (wéi, "soft leather"). This combination intuitively suggests the idea of surrounding something, much like enclosing soft leather around an object.
  - **simplification:** 圍 → 围(圍): 囗 (wéi, "enclosure") was simplified by removing the internal component 韋 (wéi, "soft leather").
- **examples:**
  - 士( )兵( )围(圍)困( )敌(敵)军(軍)。
    - Shìbīng wéikùn díjūn.
    - Soldiers surrounded the enemy army.
  - 村( )民( )围(圍)绕(繞)湖( )边(邊)举(舉)行( )庆(慶)典( )。
    - Cūnmín wéirào húbiān jǔxíng qìngdiǎn.
    - Villagers held a celebration around the lake.
  - 老( )师(師)围(圍)着(著)学(學)生( )讲(講)解( )科( )学(學)。
    - Lǎoshī wéizhe xuéshēng jiǎngjiě kēxué.
    - The teacher explained science while gathering the students around.
### 围(圍) → 囗
- **definition:** enclosure
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an enclosure
  - **interpretation:** The character 囗 (wéi, 'enclosure') is a pictogram representing a square or rectangular enclosure, emblematic of walls or boundaries. It visually reflects a basic enclosed area delineated by straight lines.
- **examples:**
  - 博( )物( )馆(館)外( )有( )坚(堅)固( )的( )囗( )，保( )护(護)着(著)历(歷)史( )文( )物( )。
    - Bówùguǎn wài yǒu jiāngù de wéi, bǎohùzhe lìshǐ wénwù.
    - Outside the museum, a sturdy enclosure protects historical artifacts.
  - 古( )城( )外( )围(圍)的( )囗( )，确(確)保( )了( )居( )民( )的( )安( )全( )。
    - Gǔchéng wàiwéi de wéi, quèbǎole jūmín de ānquán.
    - The ancient city's enclosure ensures the residents' safety.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 囗](@media/glyph56d7.png)
### 围(圍) → 韋
- **definition:** soft leather
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **components:**
  - 舛
    - chuǎn
    - footsteps
  - 囗
    - wéi
    - enclosure
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 舛 (footsteps) + 囗 (enclosure) ->
    - footsteps around an enclosure ->
    - originally for 圍 (to surround); phonetically borrowed for 'soft leather'
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 舛 (footsteps) and 囗 (enclosure) to depict the idea of footsteps moving around an enclosed area, which was originally associated with the concept of surrounding. This shape was later borrowed for its phonetic value to mean 'soft leather,' as the structural composition resembles a process of encasing or wrapping, similar to the treatment of leather.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)件( )夹(夾)克( )是( )用( )韦(韋)材( )料( )制(製)成( )的( )。
    - Zhè jiàn jiákè shì yòng wéi cáiliào zhìchéng de.
    - This jacket is made from soft leather material.
  - 古( )代( )的( )盔( )甲( )常( )以( )韦(韋)作( )装(裝)饰(飾)。
    - Gǔdài de kuījiǎ cháng yǐ wéi zuò zhuāngshì.
    - Ancient armor was often decorated with soft leather.
  - 他( )的( )书(書)包( )用( )韦(韋)边(邊)制(製)成( )。
    - Tā de shūbāo yòng wéi biān zhìchéng.
    - His backpack is made with soft leather edges.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 韋](@media/glyph97cb.png)
### 围(圍) → 韋 → 舛
- **definition:** footsteps
- **pinyin:** chuǎn
- **components:**
  - 夊
    - suī
    - foot; walk slowly
  - 𡕒
    - wěi
    - foot; part of an ancient form
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 夊("foot") + 𡕒("foot") =
    - two feet facing the same direction
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicted two feet facing the same direction, indicative of alignment or a specific movement. This contrasts with similar characters where feet face different directions, suggesting divergence or a change in direction. The character captures the concept of feet in synchronized motion, highlighting its thematic link to physical orientation.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )计(計)划(劃)总(總)是( )出( )点(點)儿(兒)小( )舛( )。
    - Tā de jìhuà zǒng shì chū diǎnr xiǎo chuǎn.
    - His plans always encounter small setbacks.
  - 尽(儘)管( )有( )舛( )错(錯)，他( )仍( )然( )达(達)到( )了( )目( )标(標)。
    - Jǐnguǎn yǒu chuǎncuò, tā réngrán dádào le mùbiāo.
    - Despite the mistakes, he still achieved his goal.
  - 为(為)了( )避( )免( )舛( )误(誤)，我( )们(們)仔( )细(細)检(檢)查( )了( )所( )有( )的( )数(數)据(據)。
    - Wèile bìmiǎn chuǎnwù, wǒmen zǐxì jiǎnchá le suǒyǒu de shùjù.
    - To avoid errors, we carefully checked all the data.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 舛](@media/glyph821b.png)
### 围(圍) → 韋 → 舛 → 夊
- **definition:** foot; walk slowly
- **pinyin:** suī
- **components:**
  - 夂
    - zhǐ
    - to go
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a footprint pointing downward; variant of 夂 (zhǐ, "to go")
  - **interpretation:** The character 夊(suī, "downward foot") visually represents a downward-facing foot, suggesting movement or trajectory in a downward direction.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )步( )伐( )缓(緩)慢( )，就像夊一般。
    - Tā de bùfá huǎnmàn, jiù xiàng suī yībān.
    - His steps are slow, like the character 夊.
  - 我( )们(們)观(觀)察( )到( )古( )代( )文( )字( )中( )，常( )常( )使( )用( )夊( )来(來)表( )达(達)脚(腳)的( )动(動)作( )。
    - Wǒmen guānchá dào gǔdài wénzì zhōng, chángcháng shǐyòng suī lái biǎodá jiǎo de dòngzuò.
    - We observed that in ancient texts, the character 夊 was often used to express the action of the foot.

### 围(圍) → 韋 → 舛 → 夊 → 夂
- **definition:** to go
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a footprint pointing down
  - **interpretation:** The character 夂 (zhǐ, 'foot pointing down') is a pictogram representing a footprint facing downward, often associated with motion or directionality. This depiction intuitively aligns with its meaning of indicating a downward step or path.
- **examples:**
  - 汉(漢)字( )中( )‘夂( )’常( )被( )用( )作( )偏( )旁( )，象( )征(徵)步( )伐( )朝( )下( )。
    - Hànzì zhōng ‘zhǐ’ cháng bèi yòng zuò piān páng, xiàng zhēng bù fá cháo xià.
    - In Chinese characters, '夂' is often used as a radical to symbolize downward steps.
  - 书(書)法( )中( )‘夂( )’的( )结(結)构(構)犹(猶)如( )足( )尖( )向( )下( )。
    - Shūfǎ zhōng ‘zhǐ’ de jiégòu yóurú zújiān xiàng xià.
    - In calligraphy, the structure of '夂' resembles a foot pointing downward.
- **historical forms:**

### 围(圍) → 韋 → 舛 → 𡕒
- **definition:** foot; part of an ancient form
- **pinyin:** wěi
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 夸
    - kuā
    - boast
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 足 (zú, "foot") + phonetic 夸 (kuā) ->
    - meaning relates to feet
  - **interpretation:** The character 𡕒 is a variant of 跨, which is constructed from the semantic component 足 (zú, "foot"), indicating its relation to activities involving feet, and the phonetic component 夸 (kuā). This combination suggests the notion of actions involving feet, such as 'stride' or 'step over', derived from the sound provided by 夸.
### 围(圍) → 韋 → 舛 → 𡕒 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )受( )伤(傷)后(後)，他( )的( )足( )不( )能( )动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小( )明( )打( )球( )时(時)，不( )小( )心( )扭( )伤(傷)了( )足( )。
    - xiǎo míng dǎ qiú shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ shāng le zú。
    - When Xiaoming was playing ball, he accidentally twisted his foot.
  - 我( )每( )天( )锻(鍛)炼(鍊)足( )部( )。
    - wǒ měitiān duànliàn zúbù。
    - I exercise my foot muscles every day.
- **historical forms:**

### 围(圍) → 韋 → 舛 → 𡕒 → 夸(誇)
- **traditional:** 誇
- **definition:** boast
- **pinyin:** kuā
- **components:**
  - 言
    - yán
    - speech
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 言 (yán, "speech") + phonetic 夸 (kuā, "boast") ->
    - boastful speech
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 言 (yán, "speech") for its semantic value, suggesting something spoken or related to words, with 夸 (kuā, "boast") providing the pronunciation. The result is a word associated with boastful or exaggerated speech.
  - **simplification:** The traditional 言 (yán, "speech") was removed, leaving only the component 夸 (kuā, "boast") as the simplified character.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )总(總)是( )喜( )欢(歡)夸(誇)自( )己( )的( )儿(兒)子( )。
    - Tā zǒngshì xǐhuān kuā zìjǐ de érzi.
    - He always likes to boast about his son.
  - 她( )夸(誇)奖(獎)自( )己( )在( )比( )赛(賽)中( )的( )表( )现(現)。
    - Tā kuājiǎng zìjǐ zài bǐsài zhōng de biǎoxiàn.
    - She boasted about her performance in the competition.
  - 老( )师(師)夸(誇)赞(讚)他( )的( )进(進)步( )很( )大( )。
    - Lǎoshī kuāzàn tā de jìnbù hěn dà.
    - The teacher boasted about his great progress.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 夸](@media/glyph5938.png)
### 围(圍) → 韋 → 舛 → 𡕒 → 夸(誇) → 言
- **definition:** speech
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 舌
    - shé
    - tongue
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 舌 (mouth with a forked tongue) with added stroke at top to suggest tongue movement ->
    - speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 言(yán, "speech") depicts the addition of a horizontal stroke to the ancient form of 舌(shé, "tongue") to indicate the motion of the tongue as it moves to articulate speech. This directly connects the organ involved in speaking to the concept of speech itself.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )的( )言( )语(語)充( )满(滿)智( )慧( )。
    - Tā de yányǔ chōngmǎn zhìhuì.
    - His speech is full of wisdom.
  - 我( )们(們)应(應)该(該)以( )行( )动(動)证(證)明( )我( )们(們)的( )言( )词(詞)。
    - Wǒmen yīnggāi yǐ xíngdòng zhèngmíng wǒmen de yáncí.
    - We should prove our words with actions.
  - 他( )说(說)话(話)的( )方( )式( )显(顯)示( )了( )他( )的( )修( )养(養)。
    - Tā shuōhuà de fāngshì xiǎnshìle tā de xiūyǎng.
    - The way he speaks shows his refinement.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 言](@media/glyph8a00.png)

## 浴巾
---
## bath towel
### yùjīn
---
- **definition:** bath towel
- **pinyin:** yùjīn
- **components:**
  - 浴
    - yù
    - bath; shower
  - 巾
    - jīn
    - towel; cloth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 浴 (yù, "bath") refers to taking a bath or shower, often associated with cleansing and hygiene. 巾 (jīn, "towel") is a piece of cloth used for wiping or drying, commonly associated with personal grooming items like towels or handkerchiefs. Together, 浴巾 (yùjīn) forms the concept of a bath towel, a specific type of towel used after bathing.
- **examples:**
  - 我( )忘( )记(記)带(帶)浴( )巾( )。
    - Wǒ wàngjì dài yùjīn.
    - I forgot to bring a bath towel.
  - 洗( )完( )澡( )后(後)，他( )用( )一( )条(條)白( )色( )的( )浴( )巾( )。
    - Xǐ wán zǎo hòu, tā yòng yī tiáo báisè de yùjīn.
    - After showering, he used a white bath towel.
  - 这(這)家( )酒( )店( )提( )供( )干(乾)净(淨)的( )浴( )巾( )。
    - Zhè jiā jiǔdiàn tígōng gānjìng de yùjīn.
    - This hotel provides clean bath towels.
### 浴巾 → 浴
- **definition:** bath; shower
- **pinyin:** yù
- **components:**
  - 氵
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 谷
    - gǔ
    - valley
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 氵 (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic: 谷 (gǔ, "valley") =
    - valley filled with water ->
    - bathe
  - **interpretation:** The character 浴 (yù, "bathe") combines the semantic component 氵 (shuǐ, "water") indicating relation to liquid and the phonetic component 谷 (gǔ, "valley"). This suggests a place where water collects, such as a valley filled with water, an apt metaphor for bathing.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )在( )浴( )室( )里(裡)洗( )澡( )。
    - Tā zài yùshì lǐ xǐzǎo.
    - He bathes in the bathroom.
  - 黄(黃)昏( )时(時)他( )在( )温(溫)泉( )浴( )池( )中( )沐( )浴( )，忘( )却(卻)一( )天( )烦(煩)恼(惱)。
    - Huánghūn shí tā zài wēnquán yùchí zhōng mùyù, wàngquè yītiān fánnǎo.
    - At dusk, he bathes in the hot spring pool and forgets the troubles of the day.
  - 她( )享( )受( )晨( )浴( )后(後)的( )清( )新( )。
    - Tā xiǎngshòu chén yù hòu de qīngxīn.
    - She enjoys the freshness after her morning bath.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 浴](@media/glyph6d74.png)
### 浴巾 → 浴 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字( )中( )偏( )旁( )氵( )，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼(魚)儿(兒)欢(歡)快( )戏(戲)水( )。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 浴巾 → 浴 → 谷
- **definition:** valley
- **pinyin:** gǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts valley: 口 (kǒu, "mouth" or open space) in between two mountain walls represented by near-parallel lines ->
    - original form is 𠔌
  - **interpretation:** The character 谷(gǔ, 'valley') visually represents a valley, with an open space flanked by lines resembling mountains. This aligns with its definition as a valley, a feature of the landscape formed by natural geological processes.
- **examples:**
  - 他( )走( )进(進)了( )幽( )静(靜)的( )谷( )。
    - Tā zǒu jìnle yōujìng de gǔ.
    - He walked into the quiet valley.
  - 清( )晨( )的( )时(時)候( )，薄( )雾(霧)笼(籠)罩( )着(著)谷( )。
    - Qīngchén de shíhòu, bó wù lóngzhào zhe gǔ.
    - In the early morning, a thin mist covered the valley.
  - 山( )谷( )里(裡)回( )荡(盪)着(著)鸟(鳥)鸣(鳴)。
    - Shāngǔ lǐ huídàngzhe niǎomíng.
    - The valley echoes with birdsong.
- **historical forms:**

![Historical forms of 谷](@media/glyph8c37.png)
### 浴巾 → 巾
- **definition:** towel; cloth
- **pinyin:** jīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a piece of cloth with two ends hanging down
  - **interpretation:** The character 巾(jīn, "cloth") visually represents a cloth or towel, with its depiction emphasizing the idea of a piece of fabric and its functionality.
- **examples:**
  - 爸( )爸( )用( )干(乾)净(淨)的( )巾( )擦( )手( )。
    - Bàba yòng gānjìng de jīn cā shǒu.
    - Dad uses a clean cloth to wipe his hands.
  - 她( )拿( )着(著)一( )条(條)巾( )，轻(輕)轻(輕)擦( )拭( )眼( )角( )。
    - Tā názhe yì tiáo jīn, qīngqīng cā shì yǎnjiǎo.
    - She holds a cloth and gently wipes the corners of her eyes.
  - 老( )人( )用( )巾( )给(給)手( )上( )包( )扎( )伤(傷)口( )。
    - Lǎorén yòng jīn gěi shǒu shàng bāozā shāngkǒu.
    - The elderly person uses a cloth to bandage the wound on his hand.
